# Canceling Your Subscription – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25384024738573-Canceling-Your-Subscription#page-container)

You can cancel your Midjourney subscription at any time by going to your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page and clicking the **Cancel Plan** button.

Your cancellation will become effective at the end of your current billing cycle, and you'll still have access to all of your subscription features—including any remaining Fast time—until then.

Canceling your subscription does not delete your generated images or account history. Any Stealth images you have will stay unpublished. You can choose to resubscribe at any time.

If you have an upgrade or downgrade scheduled, make sure to cancel that change first by using the **Cancel Change** button before you proceed with canceling your subscription.

![web-cancel.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33594632294541)

---

# Requesting a Refund – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25386088618253-Requesting-a-Refund#page-container)

You're eligible for a refund only if you've used less than 20 GPU minutes throughout the lifetime of your account. This includes both Fast/Turbo and Relax time.

If you qualify for a refund, you'll automatically see the option to request one when you [cancel your subscription](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25384024738573)
. If you don't see the refund option, we're unable to provide a refund.

Refund processing may take up to 10 business days, depending on your bank's processing times, but you'll receive a refund confirmation email from Midjourney within a few minutes.

Before requesting a refund, make sure to cancel any other plan changes you have scheduled using the **Cancel Change** button.

If you encounter any error messages, wait an hour and try again—your renewal payment might still be processing. If the issue persists, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

![web-cancel.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33594695299853)

---

# Editing Your Payment Information – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25385791792781-Editing-Your-Payment-Information#page-container)

**Active Subscription:** To review or update your payment details on an active subscription, go to your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com. Make sure you're logged in if you haven't done so already.

From there, click the "Edit Billing" button. This opens your billing portal in a new window. Inside the portal, you can add new card details by clicking "Add a payment method." Click the ... (ellipsis) button to set a card as your default payment method. If you need to delete a payment method, use the X button, but remember you must keep at least one payment method on file as long as your subscription is active.

For smooth transactions, ensure your billing address matches the address on file with your credit card issuer. This helps avoid any [unsuccessful payments](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801964045)
. 

![edit-billing.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33582583894029)

**Inactive Subscription:** If your subscription has ended, you won't see an "Edit Billing" button on your Manage Subscription page. Instead, enter your email address [here](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
. You will receive an email with a link to access your billing portal within a few minutes. Make sure to check your spam folder if you don't receive it right away.

Please note, if you also have a subscription to Midjourney Magazine using the same email address, the form might send you a link to your magazine subscription billing portal instead. If this occurs, or if you encounter any other issues accessing your billing history, please [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

---

# Unsuccessful Payments – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801964045-Unsuccessful-Payments#page-container)

When a payment is declined, you will often see a pending transaction in your bank account. This is normal, and will go away automatically. It does not mean the payment was successful. When your payment is successful you will always receive an email from Midjourney with your receipt and invoice.

Payments can fail for a variety of reasons. If you're having trouble making a payment, try please these troubleshooting steps:

*   **Check Card Information:** Ensure that all card details, including your name, card number, CVC, and expiration date, are entered correctly.
    
*   **Verify Billing Address:** Make sure your billing address matches what's on file with your card issuer. Even small differences in the address can cause payment issues.
    
*   **Funds and Limits:** Confirm that you have enough funds in your account and haven’t hit any spending limits that may be set on your card.
    
*   **Bank Approvals:** If everything seems correct, your bank might still be declining the transaction. You can call the number on the back of your card and ask for Midjourney transactions to be whitelisted.
    
*   **Try Another Card:** If possible, use a different card to try making the payment again.
    

If you've reviewed all your billing info and contacted your bank but still face payment issues, please [reach out to our billing support team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
.

---

# Reporting an Unauthorized Charge – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868804543885-Reporting-an-Unauthorized-Charge#page-container)

If you believe your card has been used fraudulently to pay for Midjourney, please [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 right away with all the following transaction details:

*   Exact amount charged (and your local currency, if it's not USD)
*   Date and time of the transaction, including your local time zone
*   The type of card (Visa, Mastercard, etc., credit or debit card)
*   Your card’s country of origin
*   Name of the bank that issued your card
*   The last 4 digits of your card number
*   The card's expiration date

**To definitively locate the charges in our system, billing support needs all of this information.**

If there are multiple charges, please provide the amount, date, and time of each charge.

Investigations into potentially fraudulent charges are a top priority for the billing team, and we can generally resolve these cases, including getting your money back to you, faster than your bank can.

---

# Fixing a Paused Plan – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868802467853-Fixing-a-Paused-Plan#page-container)

If your subscription doesn't renew because of a payment failure, your plan will be marked as "Paused". This means that the renewal payment didn't go through successfully.

You should receive an email notifying you that the payment attempt was unsuccessful. Our system automatically retries the payment multiple times over several days. However, if none of these attempts work, your subscription will be automatically canceled.

When a payment is declined, you will often see a pending transaction in your bank account. This is normal, and will go away automatically. It does not mean the payment was successful. When your payment is successful you will always receive an email from Midjourney with your receipt and invoice.

#### How to Fix a Paused Plan:

1.  To immediately stop the payment attempts, visit your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
     page (make sure you're logged in) and cancel the paused plan.
2.  Once canceled, you can re-subscribe from the same page. To update your payment information, use the "Edit Billing" button.

For more details on why your payment might not have gone through, see our [Unsuccessful Payments](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801964045)
 article. If you're still experiencing payment issues, please [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for further assistance.

![web-paused-plan.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33594323137805)

---

# Payment Currency – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868831424525-Payment-Currency#page-container)

Midjourney accepts payments exclusively in US Dollars (USD).

If you're paying with a currency other than USD, your bank will automatically convert your payment to USD. This process will involve your bank's conversion rates, and depending on your account terms, they may also charge a foreign transaction fee.

**Please note that Midjourney has no control over the conversion rates or any bank fees applied.** If you have questions concerning how your bank manages foreign transactions, it's a good idea to contact them before subscribing to understand what to expect.

---

# Tax / VAT Charges – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801261325-Tax-VAT-Charges#page-container)

When you purchase a Midjourney subscription, sales tax or Value Added Tax (VAT) may apply, depending on your location. Stripe, our payment processor, calculates your tax rate at checkout using your billing information. Any taxes due are added to your subscription price, and you'll see the total amount before you complete your payment.

This process is automated based on your billing details. Our billing support team cannot modify the taxes charged for your subscription. However, if you're part of an organization that should be tax-exempt, please refer to our [Requesting a Tax Exemption](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868838932621)
 article for guidance.

Note: Tax requirements may change over time. Just because your past purchases were tax-free doesn’t mean future purchases will be as well.

---

# Reporting a Duplicate Charge – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868806085517-Reporting-a-Duplicate-Charge#page-container)

If you haven’t received multiple receipts by email, it’s likely you haven’t been charged more than once. Often, failed payments show up as pending authorizations on your card for several days, which might also trigger payment alerts. If you've only gotten one email receipt, the extra transactions you're seeing are probably pending authorizations that will vanish automatically within a few days.

However, if you have received multiple email receipts, please [contact our billing support team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 right away.

To help us resolve the issue swiftly, include the invoice or receipt number from each receipt you’ve received. You can find these numbers in the subject line of your receipt emails or near the top left corner of the PDF versions of your receipts or invoices. Invoice numbers look like ABC1DEF2-0001, and receipt numbers like 1234-5678-9012.

---

# Accepted Payment Methods – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868831972365-Accepted-Payment-Methods#page-container)

Midjourney uses Stripe as our payment processor, which means you can only use payment methods that Stripe accepts. Generally, you can pay with major credit and debit cards like Visa, Mastercard, and American Express, as well as some digital wallets such as Apple Pay, Amazon Pay, Alipay, Google Pay, and Link in some regions. The options you see during checkout are the ones available to you.

We can only accept the payment methods shown at checkout, and our billing support team can't help set up any alternatives unless you're [buying in bulk as a company](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870607078285)
.

Unfortunately, PayPal isn't currently supported.

Stripe is a PCI Service Provider Level 1, the most stringent level of certification available in the payments industry.

---

# Viewing Your Payment History – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868885185293-Viewing-Your-Payment-History#page-container)

All your invoices and receipts are automatically emailed to the billing email address on file, so you might also find them in your inbox.

**Active Subscription:** If you have an active subscription, accessing your billing history is straightforward. Log in to midjourney.com and navigate to the [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page. Once there, click the "View Invoices" button to open your billing portal in a new window. At the bottom of this page, you’ll find your Invoice History, where you can click on any invoice to view it.

![view-invoices.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33582880781197)

**Inactive Subscription:** If your subscription has ended, you won't see a "View Invoices" button on your Manage Subscription page. Instead, enter your email address [here](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
. You will receive an email with a link to access your billing portal within a few minutes. Make sure to check your spam folder if you don't receive it right away.

Please note, if you also have a subscription to Midjourney Magazine using the same email address, the form might send you a link to your magazine subscription billing portal instead. If this occurs, or if you encounter any other issues accessing your billing history, please [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

---

# Changing Your Invoice Information – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868825749517-Changing-Your-Invoice-Information#page-container)

The name, physical address, and VAT or Tax ID that you have in your Stripe payment details are what appear on your invoice. To update this information, you can simply [edit your payment details.](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25385791792781)

Bear in mind that any changes you make will apply only to future invoices. Unfortunately, we cannot change invoices that have already been issued, so ensure that the payment details you enter at checkout are the ones you want to see on your invoice.

---

# Requesting a Tax Exemption – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868838932621-Requesting-a-Tax-Exemption#page-container)

This article is for Midjourney subscribers from tax-exempt organizations paying for their subscription. Please note that we cannot modify tax status for individual users. If you're an individual, refer to our other article on [how taxes are determined for your subscription](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801261325)
.

When Subscribing
----------------

During checkout, tick the "I'm purchasing as a business" box that will appear after you enter your payment and address information, if taxes apply. This will reveal fields for entering your tax ID, like an EIN in the United States or a VAT number in applicable countries. This information will appear automatically on future invoices.

Our payment processor will try to validate your tax status and apply any eligible exemptions. If the option doesn’t appear, or if validation fails, you can [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 after subscribing to update your account and refund any taxes charged.

![tax-id-stripe.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33595796930573)

After Subscribing
-----------------

To request a tax exemption or reverse-charge status, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 with the following details:

*   Full name on your account
*   Billing email address
*   Physical billing address
*   For VAT countries: Company’s VAT number
*   For non-VAT countries: Tax-exempt status documentation, such as a tax exemption certificate

Ensure your subscription’s billing information matches your exemption documentation. Once we confirm your tax status, we’ll update your account and refund any taxes paid for the current calendar year.

Please note: Billing support can only adjust tax status post-subscription. Processing tax exemption requests may take up to two weeks. We cannot alter past invoices, but your updated info will show on future ones.

---

# Turning Off Automatic Renewals – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868888211213-Turning-Off-Automatic-Renewals#page-container)

All Midjourney subscriptions are set to renew automatically. If you'd prefer not to continue your subscription, you can cancel it via your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com. Be sure to log in first if you’re not already.

Once you cancel, you'll still enjoy your current plan’s features and any remaining GPU time until your subscription period ends. However, the plan won't automatically renew at the end of your billing period. Remember, each time you subscribe, you'll need to cancel before renewal if you don't want it to auto-renew—disabling automatic renewals entirely isn't an option.

Canceling comes without penalties, and all your images created with Midjourney will remain saved in your account. You can access them anytime on midjourney.com, even without an active subscription.

![web-cancel.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33581617374733)

---

# Discord Nitro Subscription – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870371412749-Discord-Nitro-Subscription#page-container)

[Discord Nitro](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/115000435108-What-are-Nitro-Nitro-Basic)
 is a Discord subscription with perks for your account, but it’s different from a Midjourney subscription. Having Discord Nitro won't give you access to Midjourney, and you don’t need Discord Nitro to use Midjourney.

When you go to the "Subscriptions" page in your Discord user settings, you'll only see Discord Nitro subscriptions. Midjourney subscriptions won’t be listed there. If you accidentally signed up for Discord Nitro thinking it would let you use Midjourney, you might be able to [get a refund from Discord](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/360012668071-Refund-Policy)
.

If you need help subscribing to Midjourney, check out our [How to Subscribe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573)
 article.

To get help with your Discord Nitro subscription, [visit Discord's support site](https://support.discord.com/)
.

---

# Changing Your Billing Email – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868854770573-Changing-Your-Billing-Email#page-container)

Your billing email is the address our payment processor, Stripe, uses to send you invoices and receipts for your Midjourney purchases. This email may be different from the one you use to log in to your Midjourney account, and changing it won’t affect your login process on midjourney.com or Discord. For more details about logging in, check out our [Logging In & Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509)
 article.

To update your billing email address, you'll need assistance from Midjourney's billing support team, so please [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for help. For security purposes, you might need to answer some verification questions to ensure your account remains safe.

---

# Free Trials – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870399340173-Free-Trials#page-container)

A limited trial is available on the [niji · journey](https://nijijourney.com/)
 app, available for [iOS](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/niji-journey/id6446376937)
 and [Android](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.spellbrush.nijijourney)
 devices. No free trial is currently available in Discord or the midjourney.com website.

See our [How to Subscribe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573)
 article for help subscribing to Midjourney.

---

# Deleting Your Data – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870397554701-Deleting-Your-Data#page-container)

If you wish to delete all personal data associated with your Midjourney account, you can initiate this process from the [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com. Locate the "How can I delete my account?" FAQ section at the bottom of the page and follow the instructions provided.

**Once you initiate the deletion, your subscription will be immediately canceled.** There is a 7-day window during which you can reconsider your decision before your data is permanently erased. Remember, once your data is deleted, your account cannot be restored. Be sure to save anything from your account that you might need in the future.

For any additional questions, please see our [Data Deletion and Privacy FAQ](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084462534541)
 policy page.

---

# Using Images & Videos Commercially – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870375276557-Using-Images-Videos-Commercially#page-container)

With Midjourney, you own all the images and videos you create, even if you decide to cancel your subscription. Feel free to use them however you like, with just a couple of exceptions:

1.  If you upscale an image that another user created, that image belongs to the original creator, not you. It will show up in their gallery on our website, so you'll need their permission to use it.
2.  If you are part of a business grossing more than $1,000,000 USD a year, you need a Pro or Mega Plan to use your images commercially for your company.

Full details can be found in the Midjourney [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
, Section 4: Copyright and Trademark.

#### Understanding Copyrights

It's important to know that Midjourney cannot offer guidance on copyright matters. Copyright laws differ from one country to another, so we recommend contacting a lawyer or legal expert if you have specific questions or concerns.

---

# Managing Your Midjourney Magazine Subscription – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870410169997-Managing-Your-Midjourney-Magazine-Subscription#page-container)

Your Midjourney Magazine subscription is entirely separate from your image generation subscription.

To manage your magazine subscription, enter your magazine billing email into [this form](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
. This is the only method for managing your magazine subscription.

Important: Any changes you make to your image generation subscription on the Manage Subscription page at midjourney.com will not affect your magazine subscription. The two subscriptions operate independently.

After entering your email in the above form, you'll receive an email with a link to your magazine billing portal.

If you encounter any issues—such as the link directing you to your Midjourney Bot subscription instead of your magazine subscription—please [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

---

# Group Plans & Enterprise Billing – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870607078285-Group-Plans-Enterprise-Billing#page-container)

Currently, Midjourney does not offer discounts or free plans for organizations, including non-profits and educational institutions.

If your organization requires 50 or more yearly Pro or Mega Plans, our support team can assist with bulk billing arrangements. Simply [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for more details.

**Please note that we do not offer the following:**

1.  Seat management
2.  Terms and policy negotiations
3.  Participation in vendor processes, such as signing organization-required forms

For needs under 50 subscriptions, please subscribe through our standard channels. Refer to our [How to Subscribe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573)
 article for guidance.

If you experience payment issues when using the same billing information for multiple accounts, [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

---

# Finding Your Renewal Time – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870433501837-Finding-Your-Renewal-Time#page-container)

To know when your subscription renews, remember that it happens exactly on the same day and time each month as when you first subscribed.

For those on a yearly plan, your plan hours refresh monthly on the same day. For instance, if you subscribed to a yearly plan on August 8, your plan hours will refresh on the 8th of each month.

To easily find your renewal date, you can either use the [info command in Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084927086861)
 or visit your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com.

Your renewal time may vary up to an hour from what's shown in Discord due to Daylight Saving Time/Summer Time.

Remember, all Midjourney subscription plans automatically renew unless you [set your plan to cancel](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25384024738573)
.

---

# Upgrading or Downgrading Your Plan – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870428114317-Upgrading-or-Downgrading-Your-Plan#page-container)

Need to adjust your Midjourney plan? You can easily upgrade or downgrade from the [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com. If you're not logged in yet, be sure to log in first. Then, scroll down past your current subscription details to view other available plans.

Use the "Upgrade Plan" or "Downgrade Plan" button under the new plan you'd like to switch to.

If you're switching from a yearly plan to an upgraded monthly plan, the website won’t allow an immediate change. Please [contact our billing support team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

*   When you move to a higher-tier plan, you can choose to upgrade immediately or wait until your regular renewal date.
    
    If you upgrade right away, you'll receive a discount based on any unused Fast time from your current plan. If all your Fast time is used up, the new plan will be at full price.
    
    Your subscription will reset immediately, granting you all the benefits of the new plan, including Fast time, and setting your next renewal one month (or one year for yearly plans) from your upgrade date.
    
    ![upgrade.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33577999132941)
    
    Some payment methods and banks won't allow you to upgrade. If you're having any trouble, please [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
     for assistance.
    
*   If you decide to switch to a lower-tier plan, the change will take effect at your next renewal, not immediately. Please note that downgrading won't [refund your current plan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/25386088618253)
    .

---

# Transferring Your Subscription – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31541557571981-Transferring-Your-Subscription#page-container)

If you’ve lost access to the Discord or Google accounts you use to log in to midjourney.com, here’s what you can do:

First, reach out to [Discord Support](https://support.discord.com/)
 or [Google Support](https://support.google.com/)
 for help in recovering your account. Sadly, Midjourney support can't help with recovering your login details for these services. If you’re unable to get access back, [contact our billing support team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance and options to recover your Midjourney account.

Just a heads-up, your Midjourney subscription and image history can't be transferred. In some cases, we might be able to offer a credit transfer if you need to subscribe using a different account. However, your image gallery, image count history, and other account-specific details won’t move with you. For any help or questions, [contact our billing support team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
.

# Community Guidelines – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109-Community-Guidelines#page-container)

### Midjourney is an open-by-default community. To keep the platform accessible and welcoming to the broadest number of users, content must be “Safe For Work” (SFW).

**We have 4 main rules**

1.  **Be kind and respect each other**
2.  **SFW content only**
3.  **Be thoughtful about how you share your creations**
4.  **Unauthorized automation & third party apps are not allowed**

Thank you for helping us make Midjourney a safe, welcoming space for everyone.

If you see someone violating these guidelines, you can report it [here](https://www.midjourney.com/help)
.

Please use these incredible powers with joy, wonder, responsibility and respect.

Rules
-----

1.  Be kind and respect each other
    1.  Be kind and respect each other and staff. Violent behavior, harassment or incitement of any kind will not be tolerated.
    2.  Do not create images or use text prompts that are inherently disrespectful, aggressive, or otherwise abusive.
    3.  Do not create or use imagery of real people, famous or otherwise, that could be used to harass, abuse, defame, or otherwise harm.
    4.  Respect others’ rights. Do not attempt to find out others' private information. Do not upload others’ private information.
2.  SFW content only
    1.  Do not create or attempt to create gore or adult content. Avoid making visually shocking or disturbing content.
    2.  What is Considered Gore? Gore includes images of detached body parts of humans or animals, cannibalism, blood, violence (images of shooting or bombing someone, for instance), mutilated bodies, severed limbs, pestilence, etc.
    3.  What is NSFW or Adult Content? Avoid nudity, sexual organs, fixation on such things, sexualized imagery, fetishes, people in showers, on toilets, etc.
    4.  Do not create or attempt to create content that in any way sexualizes children or minors. This includes real images as well as generated images. Do not generate, upload, share, or make attempts to distribute content that depicts, promotes, or attempts to normalize child sexual abuse.
    5.  Do not create other offensive content. Other things may be deemed offensive or abusive because they can be viewed as racist, homophobic, disturbing, or in some way derogatory to a community. This includes offensive or inflammatory images of celebrities or public figures.
3.  Be thoughtful about how you share your creations
    1.  Do not publicly repost the creations of others without their permission.
    2.  Be careful about sharing. It’s okay to share your creations outside of the Midjourney community, but please consider how others might view your content.
    3.  Do not generate images to spread misinformation or disinformation.
    4.  Do not generate images for political campaigns or to try to influence the outcome of an election.
    5.  Do not generate images to attempt to or to actually deceive or defraud anyone.
    6.  Do not intentionally mislead recipients of generated images about their nature or source.
4.  Unauthorized automation and third party apps are not allowed
    1.  In order to maintain the highest quality experience for all users, Midjourney accounts are designed for individual use and each user may maintain only one account.
    2.  With a few rare exceptions that are explicitly granted, Midjourney does not provide an API, nor provide third-party apps or scripts, and automating interactions with Midjourney service is strictly prohibited according to our Terms of Service. Accounts who do not comply with these rules may be blocked.
    3.  You may not resell or redistribute Midjourney Services or access to the Service (this includes sharing your account).
5.  Moderation Policy Notes
    1.  Midjourney will block some text and image inputs automatically. An input not being automatically blocked does not necessarily mean that it is allowed.
    2.  Users who violate the Terms of Service may be warned by a community moderator, given a time-out, or be blocked from the service.
    3.  If you see someone else’s content that breaks the rules, please report it.
6.  Overall Policy Notes
    1.  The above rules apply to all content, including images made in private servers, images deleted/hidden, using Stealth Mode, in direct messages with the Midjourney Bot, and Midjourney websites.
    2.  Any violations of these rules may lead to bans from our services.
    3.  Midjourney is both a product and community. We may revoke your access to the community separately from access to the product.
    4.  Content guidelines are continually reviewed and may be modified as the Midjourney community grows.
    5.  Do not generate images for illegal activity or upload images to our servers that involve illegal activity, or where the uploading itself may be illegal.
    6.  This is not an exhaustive list. We may take action against users that violate the spirit of these guidelines, even if their actions are not explicitly prohibited.
    7.  We are a small team striving to balance the needs of the broadest number of users in our community. Our decision making process is not a democracy, but we take feedback on moderation very seriously.
    8.  Most importantly, have fun!

Specific Community Guidelines & Important Reminders for Editor
--------------------------------------------------------------

The Editor is a powerful new tool for unleashing imagination. It’s not for creating images that might deceive, harass, or maliciously harm others.

*   Do not abuse the Editor to manipulate images of real people, famous or otherwise, in ways that could lead to harassment, abuse, or harm.
*   Do not abuse the Editor to create images intended to offend, deceive, or maliciously harm others.
*   Do not abuse the Editor to create NSFW or sexualized imagery. We will take especially strict action against anyone attempting to produce sexualized images of real people.

Anyone attempting to violate our Community Guidelines using the Editor will face suspension or banning without refund. Use this tool with respect and consideration for others.

Self-Policing & Reporting
-------------------------

Occasionally prompts will unintentionally produce not safe for work content. Please self-police these images by using the ❌ emoji reaction or by right-clicking selecting Apps and then clicking Cancel Job to delete the image in Discord.

Users may flag any image for moderator review by right-clicking selecting Apps, and then clicking Report Job within Discord or the website by selecting the Options ![options-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33734790404877) button under an image and clicking Report.

*   ![web-report.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33734790406413)
*   ![MJ_Report_App.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32015016592397)

---

# Midjourney Magazine Subscription FAQ – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/28012940139021-Midjourney-Magazine-Subscription-FAQ#page-container)

This FAQ applies to Midjourney Magazine subscriptions. If you have questions about individual orders placed on [mag.midjourney.com](https://mag.midjourney.com/)
 for past issues or books, see the [Midjourney Store Orders FAQ](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/28012925933837)
 instead.

#### When will I receive my magazine issues?

Midjourney Magazine ships monthly, towards the end of each month. When you subscribe, your first issue will be the one that ships near the end of the following month. For example, if you subscribe in June, your first issue will be shipped at the end of July. Shipping times can vary from 1 to 6 weeks, depending on your location.

| Issue | Payment | Issue Deadline | Estimated Ship Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 25  | March 1-31 | March 31 | End of April |
| 26  | April 1-30 | April 30 | End of May |
| 27  | May 1-31 | May 31 | End of June |
| 28  | June 1-30 | June 30 | End of July |
| 29  | July 1-31 | July 31 | End of Aug |
| 30  | Aug 1-31 | Aug 31 | End of Sept |
| 31  | Sept 1-30 | Sept 30 | End of Oct |

#### How do magazine subscriptions ship?

To keep costs low, magazine issues ship without tracking, using slower shipping methods. Please allow up to 6 weeks for delivery after shipping. Magazines for North America, South America, Australia, and parts of Asia are shipped from Canada, while deliveries to Europe, the Middle East, Africa, and other parts of Asia ship from the UK.

#### How can I change my shipping address?

To update your shipping address, enter your billing email into the [magazine subscription portal](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
 and follow the link sent to your email. You must make changes by the last day of each month for them to apply to the next month's issue shipment. If you encounter any issues with the portal, such as being redirected to your Midjourney image generation subscription, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

#### How can I view and manage my magazine subscription?

Your magazine subscription is separate from your image generation subscription. Manage it by entering your billing email in the [magazine subscription portal](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
 and using the access link sent to your inbox. For issues accessing the portal, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for help.

#### How do I cancel my magazine subscription?

To cancel, enter your billing email in the [subscription portal](https://billing.stripe.com/p/login/aEUdRA5Wc8t25a03cc)
, and use the link to access your account. Click "Cancel Plan" to stop future issues. Any issues you’ve already paid for will still be sent. If issues arise during this process, [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
.

#### Can I order multiple copies of the magazine?

You can subscribe up to four times to receive extra copies of each issue. For past issues, visit [mag.midjourney.com](https://mag.midjourney.com/)
, but note that stock may be limited.

#### Can I get copies of Midjourney Magazine for my group?

We reserve copies for schools, stores, and community groups monthly. To apply for our distribution list, please fill out [this form](https://mag.midjourney.com/distribution)
. Please be aware that you may be responsible for customs/duties/import fees and brokerage fees payable to the shipping carrier prior to delivery.

#### Is there a digital version of the magazine?

No digital version is available. The magazine celebrates community creativity through print, offering a pause from screen time to enjoy art at a different pace.

#### How are images chosen? Can I submit an image for the magazine?

We compile the top-rated community images on Midjourney, shortlist a few hundred, and publish select ones based on criteria such as clarity, originality, and composition. Direct submissions are not accepted.

#### What if I don't receive my magazine, or it arrives damaged?

If your magazine hasn’t arrived within 6 weeks post-shipping, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
. Remember, issues ship at the end of the month following your payment and may take 1 to 6 additional weeks for delivery.

We do our best to protect the magazines by having them wrapped in plastic for shipping, but unfortunately damage can sometimes still happen. 

#### How can I get more help?

For any other magazine subscription concerns, [contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 for assistance.

# Subscription Fast Time Expiration – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870521824653-Subscription-Fast-Time-Expiration#page-container)

Keep in mind that any unused [Fast time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
 from your subscription will not carry over to the next month. Whether you're on a monthly or yearly plan, unused Fast time vanishes at the end of each month, so be sure to use it up before the month ends!

To know when your current subscription month ends, check out our [Finding Your Renewal Time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870433501837)
 article.

---

# Midjourney Store Orders FAQ – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/28012925933837-Midjourney-Store-Orders-FAQ#page-container)

This FAQ applies to orders placed on [mag.midjourney.com](https://mag.midjourney.com/)
 for past issues or books. If you have questions about your monthly Midjourney magazine subscription, see the [Midjourney Magazine Subscription FAQ](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/28012940139021)
 instead.

General Order Questions
-----------------------

#### Can orders be edited after they're placed?

Unfortunately, once an order is placed, we can't modify the items. However, if you need to cancel your order or update your shipping address, we might be able to assist. See below for more details.

#### Can orders be canceled and refunded after they're placed?

Orders that haven't yet been processed may be cancelable. [Contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 as soon as possible for the best chance of canceling your order.

#### Can shipping addresses be changed after an order is placed?

We can potentially update your address before the order ships. [Contact billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 as soon as possible to increase the likelihood of a successful change.

#### If an issue is sold out, when will it be restocked?

At this time, there are no plans to restock any sold-out issues.

#### What if my store order is missing or damaged?

If your order is missing or damaged, [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 within 30 days of your order date, and we'll gladly assist you.

#### Are customs fees and taxes included in the price?

No, you'll be responsible for additional customs/duties/import fees and brokerage fees payable to the shipping carrier based on your location, prior to delivery.

#### Do packages ship with tracking?

Individual magazine issue orders do not include tracking unless the order includes a Midjourney Year One book, or if shipping multiple issues/copies internationally. You'll receive a shipment confirmation email with the tracking number if available once your order ships.

#### Can I get an invoice for orders from the store?

We can't generate invoices for orders made through the Midjourney Store, but a receipt should be emailed to you automatically.

Year One Book Questions
-----------------------

#### When will I receive my Midjourney Year One book?

Orders typically ship within 2 business days, excluding holidays. Delivery generally takes 5-7 business days within the United States and Canada, and 1-2 weeks for international orders. You'll receive a confirmation email with a tracking number once shipped.

#### Does the Midjourney Year One book ship internationally?

Yes, Midjourney Year One ships to most parts of the world. Please note that international delivery may take several weeks.

#### How do Midjourney Year One books ship?

Year One books ship with tracking. A tracking number will be emailed to you once your order ships. United States deliveries are via USPS, Canadian deliveries via Canada Post, and international orders via FedEx or UPS.

#### Is there a digital version of the book?

No, Midjourney Year One is a physical book intended to celebrate our progress as a technical team and creative community.

#### What if my book is missing or damaged?

If your order is missing or damaged, [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
 within 30 days of your order date, and we'll gladly assist you.

---

# Using Midjourney in Discord – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31541509949069-Using-Midjourney-in-Discord#page-container)

All our [subscription plans](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870484040333)
 allow you to use Midjourney both on our website and in Discord. But if you want to make images in Discord, you will need to have a Discord account connected to your Midjourney account. You can do this on your [Account Settings](https://www.midjourney.com/profile-settings)
 page on midjourney.com

You will not be able to connect a Discord account to your current subscription if that Discord account has been used in the past to make images with Midjourney. For more information see our [Logging In & Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509)
 article.

![manage-profile-connect-discord.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33578346615309)

Use the "Connect Discord" button and you'll be prompted to log into your Discord account and Authorize the connection to Midjourney. 

Important: Double-check the email address associated with your Discord account. Entering an email that isn't linked to a Discord account will prompt Discord to take you through the steps of creating a new account. This could lead to complications if you already have an account. Before clicking "Authorize," double-check that your correct Discord username is shown at the top of the popup. If the username is incorrect, use the "Not you?" link.

Once your Discord account is connected, you'll see your login email and Discord username displayed on your Manage Profile page, and you'll be able to generate images in Discord.

#### Disconnecting Accounts

Accounts can only be disconnected by our billing support team. If you need help with this, please [reach out to billing support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
. You may be required to verify your account ownership before your login method can be disconnected. Your account must have one method connected at all times, so make sure you have a secondary method already connected before contacting support.

---

# Midjourney Trademark Policy – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084281102349-Midjourney-Trademark-Policy#page-container)

Last Updated: August 7, 2023

The goal of this policy is to protect customers by making it easy to readily identify products and services from Midjourney, Inc. Please read on to learn when and how you can properly use our logo, name, and other brand features (collectively, the “Midjourney Trademarks”).

What are the Midjourney Trademarks?
-----------------------------------

The Midjourney Trademarks include, but are not limited to, the following:

MIDJOURNEY™,  
NIJI JOURNEY™,  
NIJI·JOURNEY™,  
にじジャーニー,  
小船,

![Midjourney_TrademarkPolicy1.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32084281099149)

![Midjourney_TrademarkPolicy2.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32084251703949)

By using any Midjourney Trademarks, or by accessing the Midjourney platform, you acknowledge that Midjourney is the sole owner of the Trademarks and you agree not to interfere with Midjourney’s rights in the Trademarks, including challenging Midjourney’s use, registration of, or application to register such Trademarks. You agree that you will not harm, misuse, or bring into dispute any Midjourney Trademarks. You may not use any Midjourney Trademarks in metatags, search fields, hidden text without Midjourney’s prior written consent. It is never acceptable to use the Midjourney Trademarks in any form that has the purpose or effect of diverting or confusing consumers.

Please review these guidelines on a regular basis, as they may be updated from time to time. Midjourney reserves the right to revoke any permission and to change or restrict any use of the trademarks if we believe that such use is in violation of this policy or is harmful to the reputation of Midjourney or the Midjourney community.

When and How can you use a Midjourney Trademark?
------------------------------------------------

Here is a non-exhaustive list of the correct ways to use a Midjourney Trademark.

*   Use Midjourney Trademarks to refer to Midjourney, its services, and products truthfully and accurately.
    *   “Created using the Midjourney web app.”
*   Use Midjourney Trademarks exactly as shown in the list above, including capitalization and proper trademark symbol ™.
*   Please include this notice when you use the Midjourney’s Trademarks in accordance with this Policy:
    *   “\[Midjourney Trademark\] is a trademark of Midjourney, Inc. We are not endorsed by or affiliated with Midjourney, Inc.”

Here are some ways you shouldn’t use our marks:
-----------------------------------------------

*   Do not use Midjourney Trademarks in the name of your business, product, service, app, publication, domain name, or other offering.
*   Do not use Midjourney wordmarks in plural or possessive forms.
*   Do not misspell the Midjourney Marks (including hyphens, spaces etc.)
*   Do not use marks, logos, company names, domain names, social media names, community names, or designs that are confusingly similar to Midjourney’s Trademarks. Deliberate misspellings and transliterations of the Midjourney Trademarks are also not permitted
    *   Ex. Midj0urney
*   Do not use Midjourney’s Trademarks to incorrectly imply sponsorship, endorsement, or affiliation with Midjourney.
*   Do not use Midjourney’s Trademarks for any illegal, misleading, derogatory, or defamatory purposes.
*   Do not use Midjourney’s Trademarks more prominently than your company name, product, or service.
*   Do not use Midjourney’s Trademarks on merchandise for sale.
*   Do not use Midjourney’s Trademarks for any other form of commercial use, unless limited to a truthful descriptive reference.
*   Do not modify, distort, abbreviate, or combine Midjourney’s Trademarks with any other symbols, words, images, or slogans.

#### Can I use one of the Midjourney Trademarks when registering a domain name?

You may not use the Midjourney Trademarks in your own domain, if that use would likely confuse a relevant consumer. You may not use the Midjourney Trademarks in your product, app, or service, except to clearly refer to Midjourney services in a nominative fashion.

#### Can I use one of the Midjourney Trademarks when naming an application or game?

You may not use the Midjourney trademark in naming an application or a game, if that use would likely confuse a consumer.

#### What if I want to plan an online or in person event concerning Midjourney or with Midjourney community members?

To help guide your usage of our trademarks, please keep in mind the following: Meetups, events, online chats outside our Discord channel, or other in person or online events that are not sponsored or endorsed by Midjourney cannot misrepresent the event as such. In order to avoid this confusion, the event planner should promote the event as an unofficial event.

Midjourney is not responsible for your experience at these unofficial events, as it is not an official Midjourney event. In order to avoid any implication that Midjourney is associated or sponsoring the event, avoid prominent use the Midjourney Trademarks (e.g., in connection with the title of the event etc.) to advertise, promote, or otherwise talk about the event.

**IMPORTANT NOTE:** Nothing in this Midjourney policy statement shall be interpreted to allow any third parties to claim any association with the Midjourney offerings or to imply its approval or support by Midjourney for any third-party products or services.

If you have any questions at all about proper usage of the Midjourney Trademarks, please contact [trademarks@midjourney.com](mailto:trademarks@midjourney.com)

# Data Deletion and Privacy FAQ – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084462534541-Data-Deletion-and-Privacy-FAQ#page-container)

Data Deletion
-------------

To request to delete your account and data, visit [https://www.midjourney.com/account](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
. Follow the instructions listed in the "How can I delete my account?" section at the bottom of the page.  
Your data will be marked for deletion, and your subscription will be cancelled.  
To avoid inadvertent data deletion, you will have 7 days to reverse your request.

Privacy FAQ
-----------

Last Updated: February 27, 2025

#### What information does Midjourney collect from users?

We collect information that you provide to us while interacting with our services. This may include personal information that could be used to identify you, such as your username, the text or image prompts that you input, public chats, IP address, billing information for Stripe, your contact information, email address, and any other information that you share with us.

#### How long is personal data stored?

We only keep the information that you share with us for as long as necessary to serve an allowable purpose under the data protection regulations that apply to you. Some of these purposes include: providing you with the Midjourney services, maintaining and improving upon these services, helping you manage your account and the features that you can access, and other purposes laid out in our Privacy Policy. There may also be legal obligations that we need to comply with that may impact how long we retain your personal data.

#### Where is the personal data on Discord stored?

Discord is in control of all data you store on Discord. Please consult the [Discord Privacy Policy](https://discord.com/privacy)
 for more information.

#### Where is the personal data that Midjourney handles stored?

The personal information you provide is stored on Midjourney servers in the US. We take careful measures to make sure that your personal information is treated securely, and that your information is not transferred to an organization or country that does not have the adequate measures in place to ensure its security.

#### Does Midjourney sell personal data?

No. We do not sell your personal information.

#### Who can submit a request to delete personal data?

If you use or have used the Midjourney services, you can submit a request to delete your personal data. Please visit [https://www.midjourney.com/account](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 and follow the instructions listed in the "How can I delete my account?" section at the bottom of the page. There is no need for you to reside in or have used our services in any particular locations.

#### How long does a data deletion request take?

Your account and associated data will be deleted within 30 days after successful submission of your deletion request. If you change your mind, you can cancel your request within 7 days of submission.

---

# Chaos / Variety – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32099348346765-Chaos-Variety#page-container)

Add variety to your image results with the chaos parameter: --chaos or --c

### Add more variety to your image results with the chaos parameter: `--c` or `--chaos`

![chaos-header2.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35302982032653)

What is Chaos?
--------------

Chaos (also called Variety on midjourney.com) lets you add more variety to the image results you get from each prompt.

By default chaos is set to 0, and Midjourney creates four images based on your prompt. If you want each image to look more different, increase the chaos value. 

You can set the chaos value anywhere between 0 and 100, but keep in mind that higher values mean the images can be quite different and may not stick as closely to your prompt, giving you unpredictable results.

Setting the Chaos Value
-----------------------

*   Add `--c #` to the end of your prompt in the Imagine bar.
    
    ![Using the --c parameter on midjourney.com](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32099884214669)
    
    You can choose a default Variety setting for all your images in the settings panel. To do this, click the settings ![Settings Icon](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32099740593293) button in the Imagine bar. Once you set it, this will apply to all your future prompts.
    
*   Add `--c #` to the end of your prompt in Discord.
    
    ![Using the --c parameter in Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32099877782029)

---

# Privacy Policy – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083472637453-Privacy-Policy#page-container)

Last Updated: June 2, 2025

1\. Introduction
----------------

This privacy policy (the “Policy”) describes Midjourney, Inc. (“Midjourney”)’s practices with respect to personal data that is collected when you access midjourney.com (the “Site”), or access or use the Midjourney services, applications, or platform through the Site, Discord servers administered by Midjourney, or by any other means (collectively, the “Services”) . Midjourney is a communications technology incubator that provides image generation services to augment human creativity and foster social connection.

As used in this Policy, “personal data” means any information that relates to, describes, or could be used to identify an individual, directly or indirectly.

**Applicability:** This Policy applies to personal data that Midjourney collects, uses, and discloses and which may include: (i) data collected through the Services, (ii) data collected through the process of training Midjourney machine learning algorithms, (iii) data collected through Midjourney websites, and (iv) data collected from third party sources. Third party sources may include, but not be limited to: public databases, commercial data sources, and the public internet. When you make purchases, we use third-party payment processors to collect credit card or other financial information. Midjourney does not store the credit card or payment information you provide, only confirmation that payment was made.

This Policy does not apply to the following information:

*   Personal Data about Midjourney employees and candidates, and certain contractors and agents acting in similar roles.

**Changes:** We may update this Policy from time-to-time to reflect changes in legal, regulatory, operational requirements, our practices, and other factors. Please check this Policy periodically for updates. If any of the changes are unacceptable to you, you should cease interacting with us. When required under applicable law, we will notify you of any changes to this Policy.

**Definitions:** Through this Policy, You, or Your means the individual accessing or using the Service, or the company, or other legal entity on behalf of which such individual is accessing or using the Service, as applicable. Company (referred to as either "the Company", "We", "Us" or "Our" in this Agreement) refers to Midjourney LLC. Usage Data refers to data collected automatically, either generated by the use of the Service or from the Service infrastructure itself (for example, the duration of a page visit).

2\. Collecting and Using Your Personal Data
-------------------------------------------

**2.1 Types of Data Collected**  
_**2.1.1 Personal Data**_  
While interacting with the Services, You may provide certain personally identifiable information that could be used to contact or identify You. Personally identifiable information may include, but is not limited to:

*   Your user name for the Services
*   Prompts that you provide (including text, images, and those generated from spoken input and summarized into text), and other content such as photos, videos, documents, and messages that you input into the Services
*   Your IP address
*   Usage Data
*   Tracking Technologies and Cookies
*   Contact Information
*   Organizational Information like your company title
*   Your Email
*   Cookies
*   Other data that you elect to send to Midjourney, such as your survey responses or information you include in communications to us

**2.2 Use of Your Personal Data**  
Midjourney may use Personal Data for the following purposes:

*   **To provide, maintain, and improve our Service,** including to monitor the usage of our Service.
*   **To manage Your account:** to manage Your registration as a user of the Service. The Personal Data You provide can give You access to different functionalities of the Service that are available to You as a registered user.
*   **For the performance of a contract:** the development, compliance and undertaking of the purchase contract for the products, items or services You have purchased or of any other contract with Us through the Service.
*   **To contact You:** To contact You by email, telephone calls, SMS, or other equivalent forms of electronic communication, such as a mobile application's push notifications regarding updates or informative communications related to the functionalities, products or contracted services, including the security updates, when necessary or reasonable for their implementation.
*   **To provide You** with news, special offers and general information about other goods, services and events which we offer that are similar to those that you have already purchased or enquired about unless You have opted not to receive such information.
*   **For marketing and advertising purposes**, including through cookies and similar technologies with your consent where applicable.
*   **To manage Your requests:** To attend and manage Your requests to Us.
*   **For business transfers:** We may use Your information to evaluate or conduct a merger, divestiture, restructuring, reorganization, dissolution, or other sale or transfer of some or all of Our assets, whether as a going concern or as part of bankruptcy, liquidation, or similar proceeding, in which Personal Data held by Us about our Service users is among the assets transferred.
*   **For other purposes:** We may use Your information for other purposes, such as data analysis, identifying usage trends, determining the effectiveness of our promotional campaigns and to evaluate and improve our Service, products, services, marketing and your experience.

2.3 Sharing of Your Personal Data
---------------------------------

We may share Your personal information in the following situations:

*   **With Service Providers, Third Party Vendors, Consultants, and other Business Partners:** We may share Your personal information with these parties in order to provide the Services to You on our behalf, monitor and analyze the use of our Services, contact You, and for other purposes stated in the Agreement. This may also include third party analytics and advertising partners that use cookies or similar technologies to help measure performance and deliver more relevant ads, where permitted by law.
*   **For business transfers:** We may share or transfer Your personal information in connection with, or during negotiations of, any merger, sale of Company assets, financing, or acquisition of all or a portion of Our business to another company.
*   **With Your consent:** We may disclose Your personal information for any other purpose with Your consent.
*   **With Law Enforcement:** Under certain circumstances, Midjourney may be required to disclose Your Personal Data if required to do so by law or in response to valid requests by public authorities (e.g. a court or a government agency). To the extent we receive a request from Law Enforcement for Your personal data, we will promptly notify You and provide You with a copy of the request, unless we are legally prohibited from doing so.
*   **With Other Parties in order to:**
    *   Comply with a legal obligation
    *   Protect and defend the rights or property of the Company
    *   Prevent or investigate possible wrongdoing in connection with the Service
    *   Protect the personal safety of Users of the Service or the public
    *   Protect against legal liability

**2.4 Retention of Your Personal Data**  
The Company will retain Your Personal Data only for as long as is necessary for the purposes set out in this Privacy Policy. We will retain and use Your Personal Data to the extent necessary to comply with our legal obligations (for example, if we are required to retain your data to comply with applicable laws), resolve disputes, and enforce our legal agreements and policies.

The Company will also retain Usage Data for internal analysis purposes. Usage Data is generally retained for a shorter period of time, except when this data is used to strengthen the security or to improve the functionality of Our Service, or We are legally obligated to retain this data for longer time periods.

**2.5 Transfer of Your Personal Data**  
Your information, including Personal Data, is processed at the Company's operating offices and in any other places where the parties involved in the processing are located. It means that this information may be transferred to — and maintained on — computers located outside of Your state, province, country or other governmental jurisdiction where the data protection laws may differ from those in Your jurisdiction.

Your consent to this Privacy Policy followed by Your submission of such information represents Your agreement to that transfer.

The Company will take all steps reasonably necessary to ensure that Your data is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy and no transfer of Your Personal Data will take place to an organization or a country unless there are adequate controls in place including the security of Your data and other personal information.

2.6 Security of Your Personal Data
----------------------------------

The security of Your Personal Data is important to Us, but remember that no method of transmission over the Internet, or method of electronic storage is 100% secure. While We strive to use commercially acceptable means to protect Your Personal Data, We cannot guarantee its absolute security.

3\. Children's Privacy
----------------------

Our Service does not address anyone under the age of 13. We do not knowingly collect personally identifiable information from anyone under the age of 13. If You are a parent or guardian and You are aware that Your child has provided Us with Personal Data, please contact Us. If We become aware that We have collected Personal Data from anyone under the age of 13 without verification of parental consent, We take steps to remove that information from Our servers.

If We need to rely on consent as a legal basis for processing Your information and Your country requires consent from a parent, We may require Your parent's consent before We collect and use that information.

4\. Links to Other Websites
---------------------------

Our Service may contain links to other websites that are not operated by Us. If You click on a third party link, You will be directed to that third party's site. We strongly advise You to review the Privacy Policy of every site You visit.

Third party sites and services (including Discord) have separate practices regarding the protection of personal data that you provide to them. We have no control over and assume no responsibility for the content, privacy policies or practices of these third party sites or services.

5\. Changes to this Privacy Policy
----------------------------------

We may update Our Privacy Policy from time to time. We will notify You of any changes by posting the new Privacy Policy on this page.

We will let You know via email and/or a prominent notice on Our Service, prior to the change becoming effective and update the "Last updated" date at the top of this Privacy Policy.

You are advised to review this Privacy Policy periodically for any changes. Changes to this Privacy Policy are effective when they are posted on this page.

6\. Supplemental Terms and Conditions for Certain Regions
---------------------------------------------------------

**Europe**  
If You are located in the European Economic Area (the “EEA”), Switzerland, or the United Kingdom (the “UK”) Our legal basis for collecting and using the Personal Data described in this Policy will depend on the personal data concerned and the specific context in which we collect it. However, we will normally collect personal data from you only where we have your consent to do so, where we need the personal data to perform a contract with you, or where the processing is in our legitimate interests and not overridden by your data protection interests or fundamental rights and freedoms. In some cases, we may also have a legal obligation to collect personal data from you.

Midjourney may share information internally or with third parties, as further described in this Policy. When we share Personal Data of individuals in the EEA, Switzerland or UK with third parties, we make use of a variety of legal mechanisms to safeguard the transfer including the European Commission-approved standard contractual clauses, as well as additional safeguards where appropriate.

Midjourney uses cookies and similar technologies for analytics and advertising purposes, including to help tailor content and ads. These non-essential cookies will only be used with your explicit consent. You can manage or withdraw your consent at any time by visiting the [Privacy Settings](https://www.midjourney.com/profile-settings)
 page. Essential cookies, which are necessary for the website and our Services to function, are always active. Please refer to our [Cookie Policy](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37012090959245-Cookie-Policy)
 for more information.

Additionally You have the following data protection rights:

*   You can request access, correction, updates or deletion of your Personal Data.
*   You can object to our processing of your Personal Data, ask us to restrict processing of your Personal Data or request portability of your Personal Data.
*   If we have collected and processed your Personal Data with your consent, then you can withdraw your consent at any time. Withdrawing your consent will not affect the lawfulness of any processing we conducted prior to your withdrawal, nor will it affect processing of your Personal Data conducted in reliance on lawful processing grounds other than consent.
*   You have the right to complain to a data protection authority about our collection and use of your Personal Data.

In order to exercise Your rights please visit [www.midjourney.com/account](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 and follow the instructions listed at the bottom of the page to delete your account and data. Survey data that you may have submitted can also be accessed and deleted at this link. To access or review your account information, please follow the instructions listed [here.](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084927086861)

**California**  
This Statement applies solely to residents of California or individuals whose information has been collected in California. Midjourney has adopted and included this notice to comply with the California Consumer Privacy Act of 2018 (“CCPA”). Any terms used in this Statement that are defined in the CCPA have the same meaning given therein.

**YOUR RIGHTS AND CHOICES**  
The CCPA provides individuals residing in California or whose Personal Information was collected in California with specific rights regarding their Personal information. The below describes your rights and how you may exercise them.

**Access to Specific Information and Data Portability Rights**  
You have the right to request that Midjourney disclose certain information to you about our collection and use of your Personal Information over the past twelve (12) months. Once Midjourney receives and confirms your verifiable information access request, Midjourney must disclose to you: (i) the categories of Personal Information we collected about you; (ii) the categories of sources for the Personal Information we collected about you; (iii) our business or commercial purpose for collecting or, if applicable, selling that Personal Information; (iv) the categories of third parties with whom we share that Personal Information; (v) the specific data points or pieces of Personal Information we collected about you. If we disclosed for a business purpose or sold your Personal Information, Midjourney must also provide separate lists that: (x) identify the personal information categories that were sold to each category of recipient in connection with sales of your Personal Information; and (y) identify the personal information categories that were provided to each category of recipient in connection with business purposes disclosures of your Personal Information..

**Deletion Request Rights**  
You have the right to request that Midjourney delete any of your Personal Information that we collected from you and/or retained. Unless subject to a certain limited exception, once Midjourney receives and confirms your verifiable data deletion request, we will delete (and direct our service providers to delete) your personal information from our records. Midjourney will notify you promptly if it determines it must deny your deletion request.

**Do Not Sell or Share Opt-Out Rights**  
You have the right to opt-out of any “sale” or “sharing”, as defined by the CCPA, of Personal Information by Midjourney. While, Midjourney does not sell your information, we may share it, for example, through advertising cookies that allow our third party partners to deliver relevant and personalized ads. You can opt-out of such sharing at any time by updating your preferences in the [Privacy Settings](https://www.midjourney.com/profile-settings)
 page.

**EXERCISING YOUR RIGHTS**  
To exercise your access, data portability, and deletion or do not sell opt-out rights described above, please visit [www.midjourney.com/account](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 and follow the instructions listed at the bottom of the page to delete your account and data (including any survey responses), or go [here](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084927086861)
 and follow the instructions listed to access or review your account information.

You may only make a verifiable consumer request for access or data portability up to two times within a 12-month period. You may make a verifiable do not sell opt-out request at any time. Any such request must: (i) provide sufficient information that allows Us to reasonably verify that you are the person about whom we collected personal information or an authorized representative thereof; and (ii) describe your request with sufficient detail such that we may understand, evaluate, and respond to it. Midjourney cannot respond to your request or provide you with personal information if we cannot verify your identity or authority to make the request and confirm the personal information relates to you. Making a verifiable consumer request does not require you to create an account with Midjourney. Midjourney will only use personal information provided in a verifiable consumer request to verify the requestor’s identity or authority to make the request. Only you or a person registered with the California Secretary of State that you authorize to act on your behalf may make a verifiable consumer request related to your Personal Information. You may also make a verifiable consumer request on behalf of your minor child.

**Response Timing and Format**  
We endeavor to respond to a verifiable consumer request within 45 days of its receipt. If we require more time (up to 90 days), we will inform you in writing of the extension period and the reason for it. Midjourney will deliver any required or requested responses or other communications in writing to you by email. Any disclosures we provide will only cover the 12-month period preceding the verifiable consumer request’s receipt. If applicable, the response we provide will also explain any reasons we cannot comply with a request. For data portability requests, Midjourney will provide your personal information in a format that is readily usable and transferable. Midjourney does not charge a fee to process or respond to your verifiable consumer request unless such requests become excessive, repetitive, or manifestly unfounded or as otherwise permitted by the CCPA. If we determine that a request warrants charging a fee, we will notify you and provide you with a cost estimate before completing your request.
