# Complete Tasks – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390759197197-Complete-Tasks#page-container)

Complete tasks on midjourney.com to earn rewards and shape your Personalization.

### Your input matters: complete tasks for rewards and Personalization!

![tasks-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33513944335885)

Welcome to the [Tasks page](https://www.midjourney.com/tasks)
 on midjourney.com! You're in for a fun experience that lets you shape Midjourney while earning some fun rewards. Let's take a look at the tasks you can explore here.

Image Rankings
--------------

There are two "Rank Image Aesthetics" tasks. One focuses on Midjourney images, and the other is about [Niji](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 images. These tasks help build your [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
 data, tailoring Midjourney to better match your tastes. 

There's also the "Curate Community Frontpage" task. This one is all about voting for the creations that will be featured on the Community Frontpage of midjourney.com. Note that this task doesn’t affect your Personalization data, but it helps highlight community favorites.

#### **How to Rank Images**

Wondering how to rank images on midjourney.com? Here's a quick guide to help you make those choices confidently!

**Aesthetics Ranking  
**You're presented with two image options. Your task is to choose the one you find most visually appealing and that stands out to you aesthetically.

This choice helps build your [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
 data, tailoring future image generations to your tastes. The Personalization Profile you are currently ranking for is shown at the top of the Image Ranking page.

Not a fan of either image? No problem—just use the Skip option to move on.

![rank-pairs.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33515002263437)

**Community Frontpage Ranking  
**You're presented with a grid of multiple images. From each grid, pick the image you believe deserves a spot on the Community Frontpage—your vote helps decide what the community sees.

If you find an image you particularly love, use the heart button to add it to your favorites. For more details about an image—like its creator or prompt text—hold the Command/Control key and click the image to open it in a new window.

![rank-frontpage.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33515002267405)

Surveys
-------

These surveys help us explore the fascinating intersection of personality and aesthetics. By sharing your thoughts, you contribute to our understanding of how different styles and preferences align with diverse personalities. Your responses shape our insights and efforts in making Midjourney more in tune with your artistic inclinations.

Community
---------

Got ideas about which features Midjourney should focus on? Rate ideas and help us shape future tools and features. We’re always moving and improving based on what our community needs the most.

Earn Extra GPU Time
-------------------

Some tasks come with a special bonus of extra [Fast GPU hours](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
. These hours give you more time to create awesome images—a little reward for your efforts!

Important: You must have an active subscription to receive and use awarded Fast time, and it expires 30 days after its awarded.

*   **Image Rankings:** If you participate in Image Rankings and end up in the top 2,000 rankers for the day, you'll earn one extra Fast hour. It's a competitive space, so keep in mind that the reward isn’t guaranteed. If you use Discord, the Midjourney Bot will send you a [Direct Message](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32637339216013)
     letting you know if you've earned the extra hour.
*   **Surveys:** Complete the surveys, and you'll be guaranteed those extra hours. 

You can easily monitor your rewards on your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page, under the "Usage Details" section. Look for "Purchased & Awarded" and hover your mouse over the hours to see a breakdown of your purchased and awarded time and expiry dates for unused hours.

Any awarded Fast time you don’t use will expire after 30 days.

---

# Draft & Conversational Modes – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957-Draft-Conversational-Modes#page-container)

Turbocharge your creative flow with Draft Mode!

### Turbocharge your creative flow with Draft Mode!

  
UPDATE: Conversational Mode now has its own button you must click to activate it, which is different than what's shown in this video. Read below for more details.

What is Draft Mode?
-------------------

Draft Mode is a lightning-fast (10x faster!) way to prototype images at half the [GPU cost](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
. It's built for effortless iteration, with the option of using [Conversational Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957-Draft-Conversational-Modes#h_01JRV2QPETCNWKVX7C0S28PEB1)
 via text or voice to have AI help you write prompts.

Draft Mode is compatible with Midjourney [version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 7.

Using Draft Mode
----------------

To activate Draft Mode, head to your Create page and click the ![draft-mode-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577185236877) Draft Mode button in the Imagine bar. 

![imagine-bar-draft-mode2.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35850645507981)

Once activated, any prompts you type into the Imagine bar will run in Draft Mode. Draft Mode images generate faster and use less GPU time, making them great for experimenting and trying out new ideas. 

You can also add `--draft` to any prompt to run it as a draft, even if Draft Mode is turned off.

Enhancing Your Drafts
---------------------

If you draft an image you like, use the "Enhance" button to regenerate it using a higher [Quality](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32176522101773)
 setting. This will produce a new set of images very similar to your draft image, but using the standard amount of GPU time—just like prompting without Draft Mode. 

![enhance-button.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577185238669)

If you really love one of your draft images just as it is, feel free to [upscale](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
 it! Just click the draft image to open it, and select an upscale option from the Creation Actions menu.

Conversational Mode
-------------------

Conversational Mode allows you to describe your ideas and images in normal, conversational language to an AI that will write prompts for you.

Click the ![rooms-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577185237773) Conversational Mode button in the Imagine bar to activate it.

![imagine-bar-conversational-mode.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35850603694989)

You can use Conversational Mode in two ways:

1.  **With Text:** The Imagine bar becomes your space to share ideas with the AI. Just type in your thoughts and press enter.
2.  **With Voice:** Prefer talking? Click the microphone ![microphone-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577175649549) icon. The first time, you might need to let your browser use the microphone. Speak your ideas, and hit the microphone icon again to stop.

You can even use Conversational Mode in other languages!

If you want to tweak or explore variations of an image in Conversational Mode, refer to specific images by saying "image 1," "image 2," and so on. For example, you can say, "run a variation of image 4."

Keep in mind that you can guide the AI and communicate what you need, but you won't be writing the prompts directly in Conversational Mode.

You can use Conversational Mode with or without Draft Mode.

---

# Managing Image Uploads – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329380893325-Managing-Image-Uploads#page-container)

Hide, unhide, or delete your uploaded images with ease on your Manage Uploads page.

### Hide, unhide, or delete your uploaded images with ease.

![manage-uploads-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33486623649805)

Every image you use with Midjourney—including in prompts and [Describe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32497889043981)
 in Discord—is stored in your personal uploads library. You'll find these images on your Manage Uploads page and in the images panel, which you access by clicking the image ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33485586942861) icon in the Imagine bar.

Other users can't see your uploads library. However, keep in mind that if you're not in [Stealth Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
, the details of your prompts—like any images and the parameters you used—will be visible alongside your creations on midjourney.com.

Your [Manage Uploads page](https://www.midjourney.com/manage/uploads)
 is a convenient tool to help manage these images, and includes two viewing tabs: Visible and Hidden. 

*   **Visible:** Images here will appear in your images panel, ready for you to use anytime.
*   **Hidden:** These images are tucked away and won't show up in your images panel, but they're still saved.

![manage-uploads-page.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33502728375437)

You can easily hide and unhide images by hovering your mouse over them and clicking the corresponding button. 

If you want to remove an image completely, use the Delete button. While the image will be gone from your uploads, it will still be linked with any prompts that used it.

---

# How to Subscribe – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573-How-to-Subscribe#page-container)

To get started with a Midjourney plan, first create or log in to your account and head over to your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page on midjourney.com.

If you need help getting logged in for the first time or want to access an old account, don’t worry! Check out our [Logging In & Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509)
 article for step-by-step help.

Pick a Plan
-----------

Once you're on your Manage Subscription page, scroll down to the plans section. Find your perfect plan and press the "Subscribe" button below it. If you're not sure which plan to choose, our [Comparing Midjourney Plans](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870484040333)
 article can help you decide.

Yearly billing is selected by default, meaning the full year is paid upfront. If you'd rather pay each month, please click the "Monthly Billing" tab before selecting a plan.

Complete the Checkout Process
-----------------------------

To complete your purchase, check out using our payment processor, Stripe. If you have any questions during this process, we've got you covered with the helpful articles below.

*   [Accepted Payment Methods](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868831972365)
    
*   [Payment Currency](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868831424525)
    
*   [Unsuccessful Payments](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868801964045)
    
*   [Requesting a Tax Exemption](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868838932621)
    
*   [Group Plans & Enterprise Billing](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870607078285)
    
*   [Contacting Billing Support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
    

Keep in mind that once your billing email is set during checkout, you'll need to reach out to our billing support team if you want to [change your email](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868854770573)
. Remember, we [can't change invoices](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27868825749517)
 after they've been issued. So, double-check that the payment details you enter at checkout are exactly what you want to see on your invoice.

Confirmation
------------

After your payment goes through, you'll get a confirmation email. This email includes both your invoice and receipt. It will be sent to the billing email you used during the Stripe checkout process, which might be different from the one you use to log in to midjourney.com.

If you return to your Manage Subscription page, you should now see that your plan is active and ready to use.

Need Help Getting Started?  
  
[Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)

---

# Discord Command List – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32894521590669-Discord-Command-List#page-container)

See all the commands you can use to interact with the Midjourney Bot in Discord.

### Interact with the Midjourney Bot using Discord commands!

[Discord commands](https://support-apps.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/26501837786775-Slash-Commands-FAQ)
 are used to create images, change default settings, monitor user info, and perform other helpful tasks. To use a command, follow these instructions:

1.  Open your Discord app and go to the message box. Make sure you are in a server or channel that the Midjourney Bot has permission to access.
2.  Type `/` in the message box. You’ll see a list of commands pop up above.  
    ![discord-midjourney-commands.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32896522175501)
3.  You can keep typing the name of a command until you see it in the list. This helps narrow down the options, just like a search field.  
    ![discord-midjourney-commands2.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35185216362637)
4.  Once you spot the command you want in the list, click it. It will show up in your message box with the Midjourney logo.  
    ![discord-midjourney-commands3.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35185216364301)
5.  Press Enter or Send to execute the command.

If you’re having trouble seeing any Midjourney commands, there might be a few things you can do to fix it. First, check if you're in a server or channel where the Midjourney Bot has access. If you’re on a private server, you’ll need to add the bot to your server first.  
Still not seeing the commands? Try these steps:  
  
**• Update Discord:** Make sure your Discord app is fully updated for both desktop and mobile. If issues continue, try uninstalling and reinstalling the app.  
**• Check Discord Settings:** Click on the gear icon in Discord to open your Discord user settings. Go to the Accessibility tab and ensure the "Use the legacy chat input" option is turned off.

Full Command List
-----------------

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **/ask**  <br>Ask Midjourney Bot a question | [**/blend**](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635189884557)<br>  <br>Easily blend images together | **/daily\_theme**  <br>Toggle notification pings for the #daily-theme channel |
| [**/describe**](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32497889043981)<br>  <br>Writes four example prompts based on an image you upload | **/docs**  <br>Use in the official Midjourney Discord server to quickly generate a link to topics covered in this user guide! | [**/fast**](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)<br>  <br>Switch to Fast Mode |

# GPU Speed (Fast, Relax, Turbo) – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741-GPU-Speed-Fast-Relax-Turbo#page-container)

### To change how fast your images and videos are made, adjust your GPU speed.

Midjourney uses powerful Graphics Processing Units (GPUs) to handle the prompts you give it and turn them into images and videos. When you subscribe to Midjourney, you're actually buying time to use these GPUs. Think of GPU time like the data you get with a cell phone plan. We offer 3 different GPU speeds to chose from: Fast, Relax, and Turbo.

Note: It's important to understand that GPU time is different from the time you're spending on our website or in Discord, and even from the actual time you wait for your creations. GPU time is only used when Midjourney is actively working to create images/videos for you.

Fast Mode
---------

When you're in Fast Mode, you're tapping into your Fast time. This is a set amount of GPU time you receive each month with your Midjourney [subscription](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870484040333)
. Each time your subscription renews, your Fast time is reset. So, it's smart to use up your Fast time before the month ends, because any unused time doesn't carry over to the next month.

To check how much Fast time you have left, head to your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page and look at the usage details. If you're in Discord, you can use the [info command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084927086861)
 to see your remaining Fast time.

#### How much GPU time does a prompt cost?

Processing one image prompt usually takes about one minute of GPU time, and one video prompt about eight minutes. But remember, different tasks can use more or less. [Upscaling](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
 images, using nonstandard [aspect ratios](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
, or older model [versions](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 might require more time. Creating [variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
 or using lower [quality](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32176522101773)
 settings often uses less.

If you need more Fast time before your plan renews, you can [purchase additional Fast time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33570952624141)
 on your [Manage Subscription](https://www.midjourney.com/account)
 page or you may be able to [complete tasks](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390759197197)
 on our website to [earn free Fast time.](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/28014817524109)

Relax Mode
----------

Relax Mode for images is only available to those with Standard, Pro, and Mega plans. When you switch to Relax Mode, you're using your Relax time, which is unlimited. This means you can create as many images as you want each month without using your Fast time. The tradeoff? Images will take longer to generate compared to Fast Mode.

Relax Mode for videos is limited to the Pro and Mega plans.

#### How Long Does Relax Mode Take?

In Relax Mode, your prompt requests wait in line to be processed as GPUs free up. This means you might experience wait times ranging from 0 to 10 minutes. How long you wait can depend on how much you've used Relax Mode compared to other users. If you use Relax Mode less often, you'll typically have shorter wait times.

#### Limitations

[Permutation](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32761322355597)
 prompts, the [repeat](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32757107922061)
 parameter, and Max Upscale (a legacy [upscaler](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
) are not available while using Relax mode. Relax Mode for [videos](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589)
 is only available on the Pro and Mega plans.

Turbo Mode
----------

Want your images super fast? Turbo Mode is for you! When you switch to Turbo Mode, you're using your Fast time. This mode taps into a special, high-speed GPU pool that can generate images up to four times faster than Fast Mode.

**Keep in mind that Turbo Mode uses double the Fast time for each image.** You can enjoy Turbo Mode with Midjourney versions 5 and later. If the Turbo GPUs aren’t available or you're on an older version, your job will switch automatically to Fast Mode.

Remember, Turbo Mode is experimental, so its availability and costs might change anytime.

Switching Speeds
----------------

Your website and Discord settings are synced. This means that if you change your settings in one place, they'll automatically change in the other—including your generation speed. Double-check your settings to make sure they're set the way you want them before you generate images and videos!

*   **With Parameters:** To override your default generation speed for a specific prompt, you can add the `--fast`, `--relax`, or `--turbo` [parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
     at the end of your prompt in the Imagine bar.
    
    ![web-imagine-prompt-speed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32018844788749)
    
    **With Settings:** You can choose a default GPU speed for all your images in the settings panel by clicking the settings ![settings-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32018685231117) button in the Imagine bar. Once you set it, this speed will apply to all your future prompts.
    
    Note: Images and [videos](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589)
     each have their own settings.
    
*   **With Commands:** Use `/relax`, `/fast`, or `/turbo` as a standalone command in Discord to switch between speeds.
    
    **With Settings:** Use the [settings command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517)
     and choose `🐢 Relax Mode` `🐇 Fast Mode` or `⚡ Turbo Mode` from the menu.
    
    **With Parameters:** To override your default speed for a specific prompt, you can add the `--fast`, `--relax`, or `--turbo` [parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
     at the end.

---

# Image Prompts – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381-Image-Prompts#page-container)

Influcence the content, composition and colors of your creations using image prompts.

### Want to influence the content, composition, and colors of your Midjourney creations? Include an image as part of your prompt!

![image-prompt-header-new.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35587202934029)

There are several ways you can use your own pictures when creating prompts with Midjourney. In this article, we'll focus on Image Prompts, but there are also [Character References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
, [Style References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
, and moodboards using [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
. You can even mix and match to get exactly what you want in your images!

What are Image Prompts?
-----------------------

Image Prompts let you guide Midjourney by including an image along with your text prompt. Midjourney looks at your image's core elements, and uses it as a source of inspiration for your new and unique image.

#### Three Ways to Use Image Prompts

1.  **Single Image Prompt ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197) + Text Prompt**  
    Choose an image similar to your vision, then add descriptive text. Your text prompt should include everything you want in the final image, rather than instructions for changing the reference image.
2.  **Multiple Image Prompts ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197)![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197) Without Text Prompt**  
    Upload two or more images _without_ text to blend them together—similar to using the [Blend command in Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635189884557)
    . This is perfect if you want Midjourney to focus on visual elements. 
3.  **Multiple Image Prompts ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197)![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197) + Text Prompt**  
    Combine several images with descriptive text for more detailed guidance. Use your text prompt to specify important details not visible in your reference images.

Using Image Prompts
-------------------

*   To add an image to your prompt, start by clicking on the image ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32042622067469) icon in the Imagine bar. This opens the images panel, allowing you to upload new images or pick from those you've already uploaded. You can even select multiple images to use in your prompt!
    
    ![web-image-prompt.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32045262768141)
    
    Click your image in the uploads library to automatically add it as an Image Prompt. You can also drag and drop your image into any of the image sections to use it in different ways. To remove your image from the Imagine bar, hover your mouse over it and click the X icon.
    
    If you want to use your images with multiple prompts, click the lock icon ![lock-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34019471058573) to keep your images pinned to the Imagine bar.
    
    **Image Reference Types:**  
    ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100733197) Image Prompt (default)  
    ![style-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211100743181) [Style Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
      
    ![character-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32211087758477) [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
     (replaces [Character Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
    )
    
*   To use Image Prompts in Discord, paste your image URL at the beginning of your text prompt. If you want to use multiple images, separate each URL with a space. To easily use multiple images without a text prompt, check out the [Blend command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635189884557)
    .
    
    ![discord-image-prompt.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32045557877901)
    
    It's important to ensure that you have a valid image URL, meaning the image should already be online. If your image is stored on your computer or device, you can [host it on Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32558957919117)
     to generate an image URL.
    

Midjourney uses Image Prompts and references as inspiration to guide new creations, not to copy them exactly. If you're looking to make precise changes on your own images, check out the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
.

Image Weight
------------

If you want more control over how much your Image Prompt affects the final image, try using the image weight parameter `--iw`.

If you don't set an `--iw` value, Midjourney will use the default setting. By choosing a higher weight, your Image Prompt will have a bigger impact on the finished image.

Remember, different [Midjourney versions](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 may have different image weight ranges.

|     | Version 7 | Version 6 | Niji 6 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Image Weight Default | 1   | 1   | 1   |
| Image Weight Range | 0 - 3 | 0 - 3 | 0 - 3 |

*   • For your prompts to work, you need either multiple Image Prompts or a combination of one Image Prompt and a text prompt.  
    • Your image file should end in .png, .gif, .webp, .jpg, or .jpeg.  
    • For the best results, crop your image to match the aspect ratio of your final image.  
    • Prompts that only use images and no text are not compatible with the `--stylize` or `--weird` parameters.
    

Need Help Getting Started?  
  
[Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)

# Discord Overview – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33330535666445-Discord-Overview#page-container)

Learn all about using Discord to make Midjourney images.

### Learn all about Midjourney's Discord features and start chatting!

The [Midjourney server](https://discord.gg/midjourney)
 is a vibrant space where you can generate images, collaborate with others, find technical support, receive official announcements, submit feedback, and engage in stimulating discussions. Our community is welcoming and ready to help newcomers get started on their creative journey. If you’re eager to dive in, be sure to check out our [Discord Quickstart guide!](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32631709682573)

Discord Interface
-----------------

#### Channel List

Explore and navigate through various channels within our server. For assistance, visit the [#support channel](https://discord.com/channels/662267976984297473/958069758211797092)
 to connect with guides and moderators. Ready to create images? Head over to the #newbies or #general channels.

#### Member List

Easily spot the Midjourney Bot and see the list of our dedicated Midjourney team, guides, and moderators. If you can't find the Member List, just click the Member List icon![member-list-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33360459296781) to reveal it.

![discord-interface.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33359713849229)

#### Server List

Here, you can access your [Direct Messages](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32637339216013)
 (top icon) and view all the servers you've joined.

#### Chat Feed

This is where the real-time conversation happens! Feel free to chat and interact with other server members in this space.

Emoji Reactions
---------------

You can interact with the Midjourney Bot in Discord by using emoji reactions. Once your images are ready, hover your mouse over the message area. A small menu will appear on the right side. Click on the "Add Reaction" button, which looks like a smiley face. This brings up a menu with emojis.

![discord-emoji-react.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33361052506381)

Using a mobile device? Long press on the message area and click the smiley face button in the menu that pops up to reveal the emoji reaction menu.

There are two emojis you can use to interact with the Midjourney Bot, but keep in mind these only work on your own images.

*   If you want to receive your completed image generation to your [direct messages](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32637339216013)
     (DMs), use the envelope emoji ✉️ as a reaction on the Midjourney Bot's message. This will send the images straight to your DMs, and include helpful details like the image's [seed number](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32604356340877)
     and [Job ID](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
    .
    
    When used on an image grid, the envelope emoji will send each of the four images separately. Be sure to choose the plain envelope emoji. If you have difficulty finding it, take advantage of the emoji search bar.
    
*   The red X emoji ❌ can do two different things depending on the status of your images:
    
    **Stop Image Generation:** If your images are still generating and you use the red X emoji, it will cancel the job. This means the images will stop processing. Use the [info command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32084927086861)
     to see your currently running and queued jobs.
    
    **Delete Finished Images:** If your images are already complete, reacting with the red X will delete them from Discord and your web gallery on midjourney.com. Keep in mind that currently this is the only way to delete images from your web gallery, and sometimes it may take a little while for the images to disappear. If you want to delete an image that you can't find in Discord or that you made on the website, you can use the [show command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
     to bring it up in Discord.
    
    Important: Once you delete images, you can’t reverse the action. So, be sure before you delete them!
    

#### Troubleshooting

If you're having trouble using emoji reactions on a job, look below the action buttons for a tiny message that says "Only you can see this." This message means your images are ephemeral. Ephemeral images are visible only to you when they first generate in Discord and will vanish when you refresh the page.

Ephemeral jobs are part of Midjourney's moderation system. They are triggered by certain words or phrases in your prompt that could result in inappropriate images. To keep things safe, these images are private to you and will disappear unless you generated them in a [direct message](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32637339216013)
 with the Midjourney Bot.

Want to make them visible to others and use emoji reactions? Just use the [show command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
. Your images will pop back into view, and you can then interact with them as usual.

---

# Creation Settings in Discord – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517-Creation-Settings-in-Discord#page-container)

Adjust your default Midjourney settings in Discord with the /settings command.

### Adjust your default Midjourney settings in Discord with the `/settings` command

![discord-midjourney-settings.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32872364395917)

Accessing the Midjourney settings panel in Discord lets you change your default settings with ease. Here’s how to find it:

1.  Open your Discord app and go to the message box. Make sure you are in a server or channel that the Midjourney Bot has permission to access.
2.  Type `/` in the message box. You’ll see a list of commands pop up above.
3.  Keep typing until you see `/settings`. This helps narrow down the options, just like a search field.
4.  Once you spot `/settings` in the list, click it. If you aren't seeing any Midjourney commands, try our [command troubleshooting tips](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32894521590669)
    .
5.  Press Enter or Send to execute the command.

![discord-settings-command.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32872375092237)

Now, look out for your settings panel; it’ll pop up right in your message feed. This is your easy-access spot to view and change your default settings—simple and straightforward!

Only you can see your settings panel and options. Even if you enter the command in a public channel, only you can view it and make changes.

Your website and Discord settings are synced. This means that if you change your settings in one place, they'll automatically change in the other. Double-check your settings to make sure they're set the way you want them before you generate images!

Settings Options
----------------

#### Midjourney Default Version

Set your default [model version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 using the dropdown menu. This is the version that will be used on all your prompts unless you specify a different one in your prompt with the [version parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
.

#### RAW Mode

Click RAW Mode to automatically add `--raw` to all your prompts. Check out our [Raw Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853)
 article for more information.

#### Stylize

The settings panel has four [stylize parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
 presets that you can use. `Stylize med` is the default. Stylize Low = 50, Stylize Med = 100, Stylize High = 250, Stylize Very High = 750

#### Personalization

Clicking this button will turn on [personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
, and `--p` will be added automatically to all your prompts. If you have multiple personalization profiles, go to your [Personalize](https://www.midjourney.com/personalize)
 page on our website to set your default profile.

#### Public Mode

By default the `Public mode` button will be highlighted green. If you have a [subscription plan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870484040333)
 with access to [Stealth Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
, you can click this button and it will turn gray—meaning you are in Stealth Mode.

#### Remix Mode

Toggle this button to turn [remix mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
 on or off.

#### Variation Modes

Set your default [variation](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
 mode to either Strong or Subtle. Strong is the default.

#### Turbo, Fast, Relax Modes

Set your default [GPU speed](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
. Basic plan subscribers do not have access to Relax Mode.

#### Reset Settings

Use this button to reset your stylize setting to medium and remove any custom suffix parameters set with the `/prefer suffix` command (explained below).

Note: You can override a default setting by manually adding the parameter with a different value to your prompt.

Custom Suffixes
---------------

Want to automatically add text snippets or parameters to all your prompts? Simply use the `/prefer suffix` command, click **new\_value**, type your text and/or parameters, and press Enter or Send to execute the command. If you are using both prompt text and parameters, make sure the parameters are entered last. You can view your current suffix in the settings panel, above the version menu.

![prefer-suffix.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32874029044493)

To remove a custom suffix, use the `/prefer suffix` command again, but press Send or Enter without clicking **new\_value**. Or you can use the `Reset Settings` button in the settings panel.

Option Sets
-----------

Use the `/prefer option set` command to help you bundle multiple parameters or text snippets into a shortcut you can use repeatedly.

In the example below we are creating an option set called "mine" that contains a chaos and aspect ratio setting.

![prefer-option-set.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32874307521293)

Once created, use it like this: `vibrant California poppies --mine`. It acts like typing `vibrant California poppies --chaos 5 --aspect 2:3`. Like a shortcut!

To create an option set:

1.  Use the `/prefer option set` command.
2.  In the **option** field, type the name of your set.
3.  Click **+1 more** next to your new name, then click **value** from the box above.
4.  In the **value** field type your text snippets and/or parameters. Remember, all parameters must go at the end of your prompt.
5.  Press Enter or Send to execute the command.

To see a list of all your option sets, use the `/prefer option list` command.

To delete an option set, use the `/prefer option set` command, select your desired option set from the pop up list, and then simply press Enter or Send.

Option sets can be used in prompts on midjourney.com, but can only be created and managed in Discord.

Your option set will "expand" wherever it's placed in your prompt. If you are using text snippets in your option sets and adding additional parameters in your prompt, make sure that all parameters are at the end of your prompt.

---

# Style Reference – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653-Style-Reference#page-container)

Match the look and feel of another image by using style references.

### Want to match the look and feel of another image? You can provide Midjourney with a Style Reference!

![style-ref-header-v7.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37412423919629)

What is a Style Reference?
--------------------------

A Style Reference is a way to capture the visual vibe of an existing image and apply it to your new Midjourney creations. It doesn't copy objects or people, just the overall style—like colors, medium, textures, or lighting—helping you achieve a consistent visual theme.

Style References are compatible with Midjourney [versions](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 6 and 7.

Using a Style Reference
-----------------------

*   To add an image to your prompt, start by clicking on the image ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035478541) icon in the Imagine bar. This opens the images panel, allowing you to upload new images or pick from those you've already uploaded. You can even select multiple images to use in your prompt!
    
    ![web-style-reference.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32181174394253)
    
    Drag and drop your image from the uploads library into the Style Reference section. To remove your image from the Imagine bar, hover your mouse over it and click the X icon.
    
    If you want to use your images with multiple prompts, click the lock icon ![lock-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34019581934477) to keep your images pinned to the Imagine bar.
    
    **Image Reference Types:**  
    ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32365787270925) [Image Prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
     (default)  
    ![style-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32181269857293) Style Reference  
    ![character-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035481357) [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
     (replaces [Character Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
    )
    
*   To use a Style Reference in Discord, start by adding the `--sref` parameter to the end of your prompt, then pasting your image URL. If you want to use multiple images, separate each URL with a space.  
      
    ![discord-sref.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32181174395021)  
      
    It's important to ensure that you have a valid image URL, meaning the image should already be online. If your image is stored on your computer or device, you can [host it on Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32558957919117)
     to generate an image URL.

Best Practices
--------------

*   **Keep text prompts simple** - Avoid adding style words that might conflict with your reference image's look.
*   **Add style words selectively** - If achieving a specific style is difficult, include descriptive words that match your reference image.
*   **Focus on content, not instructions** - Use your text prompt to describe what you want to see, not how Midjourney should modify the reference image.

#### ![thumb-down-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035477645) Bad Prompt Examples:

![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035478541) the look of this image but a dog  
![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035478541) copy this style and make a bunny

#### ![thumb-up-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180011127821) Good Prompt Examples:

![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035478541) detailed portrait of a dog  
![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32180035478541) ballpoint pen sketch of a bunny

Style Weight
------------

The style weight parameter `--sw`, allows you to control how strongly the style of your reference influences your new image. You can set this parameter to any value between 0 and 1000, with the default being `--sw 100`. With the V7 model update, you may notice that style weight has more impact when used with sref codes than with images.

![style-ref-weights.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33726060931981)

Random Styles & Codes
---------------------

The Style Reference feature has been updated for V7 and old sref codes may not produce the same styles anymore. To use old codes, add `--sv 4` to your prompt (uses the old V7 model) or switch to V6.

Use `--sref random` in your prompt and Midjourney will select a preset style from its internal library at random. After submitting your prompt, "random" converts to a numerical code (an sref code), which you can reuse for the same style in future prompts.

Once your prompt has an sref code, using rerun/reroll or variations keeps the same code and style. If you use `--sref random` with a [permutation](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32761322355597)
 or [repeat](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32757107922061)
 prompt, each image will have a different style and code.

You can still use the `--sw` parameter with codes to adjust the influence of the random style on your image. You can also mix codes by using more than one, and combine images with codes.

Currently sref codes are only available for the random styles from Midjourney's internal library. You cannot create an sref code based on an uploaded image. See the [instructions above](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653-Style-Reference#h_01JCRMPT77EVWXDF6X1DG95BK0)
 to use an uploaded image. 

*   There are six versions of the Style Reference feature in Midjourney version 7 when using images. Use the `--sv` parameter to choose between them.
    
    `--sv 6` is default.  
    `--sv 4` is the old V7 sref model (prior to June 16, 2025).
    
    Each version offers a unique way of interpreting and applying your Style Reference, so experiment and see what works best for you!
    
    Note: Sref random and sref codes are only compatible with `--sv 4` and `--sv 6`
    
    ![style-ref-versions-v7.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37415853030029)
    

*   There are four versions of the Style Reference feature in Midjourney version 6. Use the `--sv` parameter to choose between them. `--sv 4` is default. Each version may offer a unique way of interpreting and applying your Style Reference, so experiment and see what works best for you!
    
    `--sv 1` The original style reference algorithm, more “vibey”  
    `--sv 2` The second iteration of style references  
    `--sv 3` An updated version of the more “vibey” `--sv 1`  
    `--sv 4` An updated version of `--sv 2`
    
    ![style-ref-versions.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34551954327181)
    

*   • For your prompts to work, you need a text prompt in combination with your Style Reference.  
    • Your image file should end in .png, .gif, .webp, .jpg, or .jpeg.  
    • Style Reference can be used with Midjourney versions 6, 7, and Niji 6.  
    • Style Reference can be combined with [Character References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
    /[Omni References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
     and [Image Prompts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
    .  
    • When using Midjourney version 6, individual Style References can also be assigned different weights: `--sref URL1::2 URL2::1 URL3::1` For more information see our article on [Multi-Prompts & Weights](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32658968492557)
    .

Need Help Getting Started?  
  
[Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)

---

# Editor – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893-Editor#page-container)

Customize your images using Midjourney's powerful tools!

### Customize your images using Midjourney's powerful tools!

![editor-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960323398541)

What is the Editor?
-------------------

The [Editor](https://www.midjourney.com/editor/new)
 on midjourney.com provides a simple and easy-to-use web interface for editing and adjusting your favorite images—both Midjourney images and your own personal ones. Use [remix](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
, inpainting ([vary region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
), [pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
, and [zoom](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
—all at once, or in any mix you choose!

When editing your Midjourney images from the Create or Organize pages, a "light" version of Editor opens, keeping you closer to your creation feed for a more seamless workflow.

If you want to upload external images or use the more advanced Editor tools, go to the ![edit-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34963807935373) **Edit** tab in the website navigation menu.

Note: Currently, images from your gallery made using [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
 can only be opened in the Edit tab. You will need to remove the Omni Reference and `--ow` parameter before submitting your edits.

Editor Tools
------------

 **![undo-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769187341) Undo, ![redo-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769191309) Redo & ![refresh-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769193613) Reset** - If you change your mind or make a mistake you can undo and redo, as well as reset all edits to start over.

![move-tool-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32764449088909) **Move / Resize** - This tool lets you move your image around the canvas, scale it by dragging the corners or using the Image Scale slider, rotate it by hovering your mouse outside the corners, and change the [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
 using the preset ratios or by dragging the gray bars on the outside edges of your canvas.

![paint-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313277837) **Paint** - Use the ![erase-tool-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769169165) **Erase** brush to select portions of your image that you want to change and regenerate. Use the ![restore-tool-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769174157) **Restore** brush to bring back areas of your original image that you erased. You can control both brush sizes with the Brush Size slider.

 **![smart-select-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313278477) Smart Select** - Use this tool to create a selection mask over parts of your image that you can erase. For more instructions on using this tool, [jump to Smart Select](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893-Editor#h_01JNSH5601AH8H973SJXKKFEV6)
. 

_The above tools are available in both the "light" version of the Editor and the Edit tab. To access the below tools, you'll need to be on the [Edit](https://www.midjourney.com/editor/new)
 tab._

![suggest-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769197581) **Suggest Prompt** - Use the power of [Describe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32497889043981)
 to generate a prompt based on your image.

**Custom Aspect Ratios** \- In the Move / Resize panel you can manually enter a custom aspect ratio for your image.

**Layers** - Add additional images to your composition using layers. For more information, [jump to Layers.](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893-Editor#h_01JQ9RW7CAN6FC6Q4GRPM0TXQP)

**Retexture** - The Retexture tool allows you to regenerate your entire image using a new style while keeping the structure and composition of the original image. For more details, [jump to Retexture.](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893-Editor#h_01JF8WA5WZ615RTPESWCCXNS2G)

**Export** - When you're happy with your edited image you can ![upscale-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950783936525) **Upscale to Gallery** or ![download-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950783941005) **Download Image** directly to your device. When downloading, you have the option to download your generated image (Save Original Generation) as well as a transparent PNG of the areas you erased (Save Current Edit).

Note: Edited images using layers and uploaded images will not be visible on your Create or Organize page unless you [upscale](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
 them.

Editor Walkthrough
------------------

*   #### Select Your Image
    
    **Midjourney Image  
    **To edit an image from your Midjourney gallery in the "light" Editor, click the image to open it from your Create or Organize page and then use the "Edit" button in the Creation Actions section.
    
    ![editor-mj-image.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960323404557)
    
    To move your image from the "light" Editor to the full Edit page, use the "Open in Edit tab" button.
    
    ![open-in-full.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36262317597837)
    
*   #### Select Your Image
    
    **Your Own Image  
    **To edit an external image, navigate to the ![edit-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34963807935373) [Edit](https://www.midjourney.com/editor/new)
     page where you have two options: you can either upload an image directly from your device, or paste an image URL.
    
    ![editor-ext-image.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313283213)
    
*   #### Resize & Paint
    
    For this example we'll upload a photo of this cute cat.
    
    To add a crown to the top of the cat's head, we first need to add enough space for the crown by adjusting the [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
    . You can do this using the Aspect Ratio presets in the ![move-tool-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32764449088909) **Move / Resize** panel, or by clicking and dragging the short gray bar at the top of the image.
    
    ![editor-resize.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960323411981)
    
    Next, use the Erase tool in the ![paint-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313277837) **Paint** panel to remove the area where the crown will sit, and add your text prompt to the Imagine bar describing what you want to see. When you're ready, press the "Submit Edit" button.
    
*   #### Results
    
    Midjourney will generate four images in the results panel. Each time you make an edit to this image, the results will get added to this panel.
    
    From here you can keep editing, or use the Export options at the bottom to upscale or download your image.
    
    ![editor-results.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960323412621)
    
*   #### Select Tool
    
    If you wanted to change the background behind the cat you can use the ![smart-select-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313278477) **Smart Select** tool to create a selection mask over areas of your image. Once highlighted, erase the area within your mask using the "Erase Selection" button. The "Erase Background" button erases everything outside your mask.
    
    Note: Make sure to apply your mask using the erase buttons before submitting your prompt. If you can still see the highlighted green areas, your mask is not yet applied.
    
    ![editor-smart-select.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313286413)
    
*   #### Retexture
    
    If you wanted to turn this image into a watercolor painting, click over to the Retexture tab and enter your new text prompt into the Imagine bar. When you're ready, hit "Submit Retexture."
    
    ![editor-retexture.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313290125)
    
*   #### Layers
    
    If you wanted to use a specific crown for the cat, you can add another image as a new layer from the Layers panel.
    
    Use the check mark in the layers panel to pick your current active layer, and then erase the areas you want Midjourney to generate.
    
    If you want to regenerate the entire image in a cohesive style, try using Retexture.
    
    ![editor-layers.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313290637)
    

Smart Select
------------

The Smart Select tool works by creating a selection mask over parts of your image. 

1.  Start by pressing the "Smart Select" button to activate the tool.
2.  Click on an area of your image to set your first positive (Include) point. This tells Midjourney where to focus.  
    ![selection-mask.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769201933)
3.  To refine the mask, add more positive points and negative (Exclude) points. Exclude points highlight areas you want Midjourney to avoid selecting.
4.  Keep adding points until your mask covers the areas you want.

When your mask is ready, choose between two options:

*   Hit the "Erase Selection" button to erase what's inside the mask.
*   Or use the "Erase Background" button to erase everything outside your mask.

Make sure to use either "Erase Selection" or "Erase Background" to apply your mask before submitting your image edits. If you need to clear the mask, use the reset ![refresh-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34950769193613) button.

Layers
------

The Layers panel allows you to add additional images on top of your original image, so you can make more complex compositions. 

To add a layer, click the "Add" button and select a new image. To reorder your layers, just click and drag them. If you need to delete a layer, hover your mouse over it and click the trash can ![trash-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960313292301) icon.

Once a new layer is added, you can use the Editor tools to make selections, erase portions, and move and scale it. Whichever layer has the check mark next to it is the active layer that the Editor tools will apply to.

![layers-panel.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35960323425293)

After you've arranged and erased your layers, you can flatten them into a single layer by submitting the edit. Once flattened, you can continue working on the image or upscale and download it.

When you submit an edit using layers, only the areas of your image with visible transparency will be regenerated (the gray checker pattern)—any visible parts will remain unchanged. To regenerate the entire image, for example in a single cohesive style, use Retexture.

Retexture
---------

The Retexture tool allows you to overlay new styles and details onto your image, while keeping the structure of the original image—like a template.

To use Retexture, click on the Retexture tab at the top of the Editor page, add a new prompt, and Submit.

If there are portions of your original image that you don't want Retexture to use, experiment with Erasing them before doing the Retexture.

![retexture.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32772821412365)

*   Midjourney provides you with powerful tools for unleashing your imagination. When using our tools to create with external images, we have additional necessary precautions you should be aware of.
    
    By using external images with Midjourney, you agree to the following rules in addition to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    
    #### External Image Guidelines
    
    *   You must meet the age requirement in our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
        .
    *   You must follow all applicable laws, our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
        , and other policies.
    *   We may remove content or restrict access at our discretion.
    
    #### Your Responsibilities
    
    *   You are responsible for all content you input, create, and share.
    *   You must have the necessary rights to use the images you upload.
    *   Do not manipulate images of public or private individuals in ways that are abusive, disrespectful, offensive, derogatory, or inflammatory—this includes sexualized deepfakes.
    *   Anyone attempting to violate our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
         will face suspension or banning without refund. Use these tools with respect and consideration for others.
    
    **If you disagree with these rules, do not use Midjourney with external images.**
    
    You will likely encounter friction with our moderation — seemingly innocent prompts may be blocked by our filters. Blocked jobs don't cost you any credits. [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
     will only be deducted when you see your results.
    
    We encourage you to use this tool and your imagination with joy, wonder, responsibility, and respect.
    
    For additional information on policies, including privacy, payments, and disputes, refer to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    

Image History & Visibility
--------------------------

Creations made in the Editor will not show up on your Create or Organize pages unless you Upscale them, but they are saved within the Editor. You can continue working on them or Upscale and Download them at any time by going back to the [Edit](https://www.midjourney.com/editor)
 page.

When using externally uploaded images with the Editor or multiple layers, both your uploads and the edited results (including Upscales) are only visible to you—they won't appear on midjourney.com for other users. These images also will not work with the [show command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
 in Discord.

---

# Discord Quick Start – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32631709682573-Discord-Quick-Start#page-container)

Get started making Midjourney images in Discord.

### Create stunning images instantly using the Midjourney bot on Discord—no special hardware needed!

• Don't be a jerk.  
• Don't use our tools to make images that could inflame, upset, or cause drama. That includes gore and adult content. See our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
 for more information.  
• Be respectful to other people and the team.

Before you jump into creating images in Discord with Midjourney, you'll need a subscription. Don't worry, the process is simple! For a step-by-step guide, take a look at our [How to Subscribe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573)
 article.

After you’ve subscribed, you’re all set to follow these steps and start making creative images in Discord. Let's get started!

Join the Midjourney Server on Discord
-------------------------------------

To start interacting with the Midjourney Bot, join the Midjourney Server:

1.  Open Discord and locate the server list on the left-hand sidebar.
2.  Press the `+` button at the bottom of the server list.
3.  In the pop-up window, click the `Join a Server` button.
4.  Paste or type the following URL: [http://discord.gg/midjourney](http://discord.gg/midjourney)
     and press `Join`.

[Learn more about Discord servers](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/360034842871-How-do-I-join-a-Server-)
.

![MJ_ServerJoin1.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32632364393229)

![MJ_ServerJoin2.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32632364401165)

Go to any #General or #Newbie Channel
-------------------------------------

After joining the Midjourney server on Discord, you'll see several channels listed in the sidebar.

![MJ_channels.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32632594849805)

**On the Midjourney Server**  
Locate and select any channel labeled `general-#` or `newbie-#`. These channels are designed for beginners to start using the Midjourney Bot. The Midjourney Bot will not generate images in other channels.

**On Other Servers**  
You can generate images with the Midjourney Bot on any Discord server that has invited the Midjourney Bot. Look for instructions on your server on where to use the Bot.

Use the /imagine Command
------------------------

Interact with the Midjourney Bot on Discord using [slash commands](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32894521590669)
. Commands are used to create images, change default settings, monitor user info, and perform other helpful tasks. The `/imagine` command generates a unique image from a short text description, known as a [prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32023408776205)
.

#### How to Use /imagine

1.  Type `/` in the message box. You’ll see a list of commands pop up above.
2.  Keep typing until you see `/imagine`. This helps narrow down the options, just like a search field.
3.  Once you spot `/imagine` in the list, click it. If you aren't seeing any Midjourney commands, try our [command troubleshooting tips](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32894521590669)
    .  
    ![discord-midjourney-imagine.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33363361714061)
4.  Type your prompt into the prompt field.  
    ![imagine-command.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33363361714573)
5.  Press Enter or Send to execute the command.

Accept the Terms Of Service
---------------------------

Before generating any images, the Midjourney Bot will prompt you to accept the [Terms Of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
. You must agree to these terms to proceed with image creation.

![MJ_TOS.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32633022241293)

Image Generation Process
------------------------

![MJ_JobProcessing.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32633001270669)

After submitting a text prompt, the Midjourney Bot processes your request, creating four unique image options within a minute. This process utilizes advanced Graphics Processing Units (GPUs), and each image generation counts towards the [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
 included with your Midjourney subscription. To monitor your available GPU time (Fast Time Remaining) use the `/info` command.

Select an Image or Create Variations
------------------------------------

Once your initial image grid has been generated, two rows of buttons become available underneath your image grid.

![MJ_quickstart_VariationUI.jpg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32633190587661)

`U1` `U2` `U3` `U4` Image Selection  
In earlier versions of Midjourney, the U buttons were used for upscaling images. With the latest model, images are immediately generated at 1024 x 1024 pixels size. Now, the `U` buttons help you separate out your chosen image from the grid, making it easier to download and giving you access to additional editing and generation tools.

`🔄` Re-run or Re-roll a Job  
The `🔄` button re-runs a Job. In this case, it would re-run the original prompt producing a new grid of images.

`V1` `V2` `V3` `V4` Image Variation  
The `V` buttons are used to create variations of the selected image. Each button generates a new image grid that maintains the general style and composition of the selected image.

Enhance or Modify Your Image
----------------------------

After singling out an image, an expanded set of options becomes available.

![MJ_UpscaledUI.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32633445064589)

`🪄 Vary (Strong)` `🪄 Vary (Subtle)`  
Create a stronger or subtle [variation](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
 of your selected image, generating a new grid of four options.

`🔍 Zoom Out 2x` `🔍 Zoom Out 1.5x` `🔍 Custom Zoom`  
[Zoom Out](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
 of your image, extending the canvas beyond its original boundaries without changing the content of the original image. The newly expanded canvas will be filled-in using guidance from the prompt and the original image.

`⬅️` `➡️` `⬆️` `⬇️`  
The [Pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
 buttons allow you to expand the canvas of an image in a chosen direction without changing the content of the original image. The newly expanded canvas will be filled in using guidance from the prompt and the original image.

`❤️ Favorite`  
tag your best images to easily find them on the Midjourney website.

`Web ↗️`  
Open the image in your gallery on [midjourney.com](https://www.midjourney.com/home/)

Save Your Image
---------------

Click on the image to open it to full size, and then right-click and choose `Save image`. On mobile, long-tap the image and then tap the download icon in the top right corner.

All images are immediately available to view on [midjourney.com](https://www.midjourney.com/)

Next Steps
----------

#### Direct Messaging the Midjourney Bot

Are you having difficulty finding yourself while working with other users on the Midjourney server? You can interact with the Midjourney Bot one-on-one in a [direct message](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32637339216013)
. Images created within your direct messages are still subject to content and moderation rules and are visible on the Midjourney website.

#### Learn More About Prompts

Learn the [basics of writing prompts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32023408776205)
 and explore how descriptions of artistic mediums, locations, and time periods change an image with [the art of prompting](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32835253061645)
.

#### Blend Your Own Images

Learn how to upload and [blend your own images](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635189884557)
 using the `/blend` command.

#### Midjourney Bot Assistance

Need help or have questions? Try these commands:  
`/help` Displays useful information and tips about the Midjourney Bot.  
`/ask` Provides answers to questions about the Midjourney Bot.

![MJ_Command_Ask.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32633669074189)

You can also visit the [#support](https://discord.com/channels/662267976984297473/958069758211797092)
 channel on the Midjourney Discord for additional assistance.

#### Billing and Subscription Queries

For billing and subscription help, please visit [Billing Support](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/categories/16016577793421)
.

---

# Web vs Discord – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329300781837-Web-vs-Discord#page-container)

Learn about the differences between making images on midjourney.com and Discord.

### Web or Discord? Compare your Midjourney experience!

With your Midjourney subscription, you have the freedom to create images on both our website and Discord. Most features and tools are offered on both platforms, but sometimes they might have different names. You can choose the one that fits your style, or enjoy using both! If you need help connecting your subscription to Discord, check out our [Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509)
 article.

Take a look at the table below to explore the key differences and similarities between making images on [midjourney.com](https://www.midjourney.com/)
 and Discord.

| Tool / Feature | midjourney.com | Discord |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Making Images with Others | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) |
| Making Images on Your Own | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) |
| Chatting with the Community | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) |
| [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384797323149) |
| [Deleting Images](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33330535666445-Discord-Overview#h_01JH6HGN86CE3MEKM57ASZEPSB) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384797323149) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) |
| [Custom Suffixes & Option Sets](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517-Creation-Settings-in-Discord#h_01JFGGQT4B34F2R6Q2CJ4FQ674)<br>\* | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384797323149) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) |
| [Publish/Unpublish Images](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)<br> (after creation) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384797323149) |
| Manage [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)<br> Profiles | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384711734925) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33384797323149) |

\*Option Sets can be used on midjourney.com in prompts, but they can only be created and managed in Discord.

Editor
------

On midjourney.com, the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
 is your go-to for making precise tweaks to your images. With everything in one user-friendly spot, you can crop, [pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
, and adjust the [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
 (and more!) all at the same time. Discord offers panning and aspect ratio changes too, but you'll need to do each step separately, which gives you a bit less control.

A standout feature of the Editor is that the [Vary Region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
 inpainting tool is built right into it. This lets you re-generate parts of your image while you make other changes, giving you a smoother creative experience.

Working with Reference Images
-----------------------------

Using your own images to guide your Midjourney creations is incredibly easy on midjourney.com. With the click of a button you can designate your image as an [image prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
, [style reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
, or [character reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
—even use it as all three! Plus, you can swiftly add any of your Midjourney creations from your gallery to your prompt without hassle. 

![web-style-reference.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33388404451469)

If you’re on Discord, you can still use reference images. However, you’ll first need to [host your image on Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32558957919117)
, grab the image URL, and then add it to your prompt along with any specific parameters. It’s a bit more hands-on, but still doable!

Reusing Elements
----------------

Mixing and matching prompt text, image references and style references is a breeze on the website. In each image's "Creation Actions" section, you'll find "Use" tools. These let you effortlessly reuse prompt text and the image itself, making it simple to craft new prompts.

![web-use.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33388825961357)

On Discord, you can achieve similar results, but it takes more manual steps. You’ll need image URLs, and you might find yourself copying, pasting, or using the re-roll 🔄 button to get everything just right.

---
