# Upscalers – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669-Upscalers#page-container)

Make your images bigger and better with Midjourney's upscaling tools.

### Make your images bigger and better with Midjourney's upscaling tools!

![upscalers-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32833059184909)

What are Upscalers?
-------------------

Once you've created an image you love, you'll likely want to make it bigger to share or save! This is called upscaling, and it takes your image to its largest size, ready for downloading or sharing. Different [versions](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 of Midjourney start with various default image sizes and offer distinct upscalers.

With the latest Midjourney version, your images start at 1024 x 1024 pixels (using the default [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
). You can then use the Creative and Subtle upscalers to bump up your images to 2048 x 2048 pixels.

If you're working with different aspect ratios, your image size will change. Check out the chart below to see how some common aspect ratios affect image sizes in version 7.

| Aspect Ratio | Initial Images | Subtle/Creative Upscale |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1:1 | 1024 x 1024 pixels | 2048 x 2048 pixels |
| 4:3 | 1232 x 928 pixels | 2464 x 1856 pixels |
| 2:3 | 896 x 1344 pixels | 1792 x 2688 pixels |
| 16:9 | 1456 x 816 pixels | 2912 x 1632 pixels |

Need a larger image than what Midjourney offers? No worries! There are plenty of third-party upscaling tools and software out there to help enlarge your images. A great place to find recommendations is our [Midjourney community on Discord](https://discord.gg/midjourney)
. Members often share tips and experiences on which tools they prefer!

Upscalers use your subscription's [GPU minutes](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
. Upscaling can take up to twice as many GPU minutes as generating your initial images.

Subtle vs Creative Upscale
--------------------------

In version 7, you have two options to upscale your images: Subtle and Creative. Both will double the size of your original image. If you choose the Creative upscaler, it might change your image a bit as it adds new details. On the other hand, the Subtle upscaler keeps changes to a minimum, preserving the look of your initial image as closely as possible.

Pro Tip: Using the Creative upscaler can sometimes help correct small issues in your image, like awkward hand positions or odd facial expressions. Plus, you can re-do the upscale more than once. Each time you do, you'll get a slightly different result. Just remember that each Creative or Subtle upscale consumes [GPU minutes](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
.

Upscaling Your Image
--------------------

*   Start by clicking on any image you've made on your Create or Organize page. This will open the image, revealing more options.
    
    Next, look for the "Creation Actions" section where you'll find the Upscale options. Select Subtle or Creative to immediately start upscaling your image. The finished result will appear on your Create page.
    
    If you can't find the Upscale options right away, just click "More options" and add a checkmark next to Upscale to make them visible.
    
    ![web-upscale.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32808216716301)
    
    Note: If your image was generated in an earlier Midjourney version, then you'll have different upscale options. More information about legacy upscalers is below.
    
*   After your image is generated, use the `U1` `U2` `U3` `U4` buttons to separate your favorite image from the initial grid. Once separated, use the `Upscale (Subtle)` or `Upscale (Creative)` buttons to quickly start generating your upscale.
    
    Note: In Midjourney versions 5 and later the `U#` buttons separate your image from the grid but do not change its size, so they do not consume [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
    . In earlier versions these buttons do increase your image size, and will consume GPU time.
    
    If you have images in Discord that were made before the release of a new upscaler, you can use the [show command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
     to "refresh" the upscale options.
    

For information about the upscalers available in older Midjourney versions, check out our [Legacy Features](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329788681101)
 article.

---

# Remix – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213-Remix#page-container)

Adjust your prompt text and guide your variations and edits using remix.

### Adjust your prompt and guide your variations and edits using remix!

![remix-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32802225214221)

What is Remix?
--------------

With remix, you can tweak or adjust your prompt text while working on your Midjourney images. When you make [variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
, use the [Vary Region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
 tool, or try the [pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
 tool, remix lets you steer how your images turn out. You can change both your prompt and the [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
 you used.

Remember, remix works a bit differently on our website versus Discord, so let's explore the details for each!

Using Remix
-----------

*   Start by clicking on any image you've made on your Create or Organize page. This will open the image, revealing more options.
    
    Next, look for the "Creation Actions" section where you'll find the Remix options. Choose from Subtle or Strong, depending on how different you want your new images to be from the original. These options work the same way they do with [variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
    .
    
    If you can't find the Remix options right away, just click "More options" and add a checkmark next to Remix to make them visible.
    
    ![web-remix.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32799537675149)
    
    After clicking one of the buttons, your original prompt and image will automatically populate in your Imagine bar with the "remix" label. From here you can edit your prompt and submit it. If you make changes you're unhappy with, use the Reset Prompt button to revert back to your original prompt.
    
    ![web-ui-remix.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37433200325389)
    
    If you'd like to change your prompt while making additional edits, click the "Editor" button. This loads your image into Midjourney's [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32696720371341)
    , where you can make multiple changes at once ([pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
    , [zoom out](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
    , remix, and [vary region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
    ). You can make changes to your prompt in the "Edit Prompt" section of the Editor.
    
    ![Editor button on midjourney.com](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32799332882701)
    
    For more detailed guidance, check out our article on the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32696720371341)
    .
    
*   In Discord, remix is a mode that you can turn on to unlock the ability to edit your prompt while performing other actions like making [variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
    , using [Vary Region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
    , re-rolling 🔄, and [panning](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
    .
    
    Use the [settings command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517)
     and click the `🎛️ Remix Mode` button in your settings panel to turn it on. You can also run the standalone `/prefer remix` command to turn the mode on or off.
    
    The default [variation](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
     mode (Strong or Subtle) in your settings will automatically be used when remixing a variation with the `V#` buttons.
    

Changing Parameters
-------------------

You can add or remove [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
 while using remix, but your parameters must remain compatible with each other. For example, if your original prompt has `--version 3` `--stylize 8000` and you change your prompt to `--version 4`, you will get an error message because the maximum stylize value for version 4 is 1000.

Only parameters that normally influence variations will work while using remix, including: [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
, [no](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32173351982093)
, [stop](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32602768934925)
, and [tile](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32197978340109)
.

Changing aspect ratios with remix will stretch an image. It will not extend the canvas, add missing details, or fix a bad crop. To adjust aspect ratios or fix cropping issues, try [custom zoom](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
, [pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
, or using the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32696720371341)
 instead.

---

# Modifying Your Creations – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329329805581-Modifying-Your-Creations#page-container)

You've generated your first Midjourney image—now what? Learn about our tools for modifying your images!

### You've generated your first Midjourney image—now what? Learn about our tools for modifying your images!

Once you've made an image with Midjourney, your creative journey doesn't have to stop there. You have a range of tools at your fingertips to modify and enhance your images. 

To get started, click on your image from your Create or Organize page to open it and reveal more options. Here's a quick look at the Creation Actions.

![image-options.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33449613222541)

If any of the Creation Actions buttons are missing, just click "More options" and add a checkmark to make them visible.

Variations
----------

![variations-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450214620301)

[Variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
 (Vary) in Midjourney let you create multiple versions of your image with subtle or strong differences. This is particularly useful when you’re happy with your original image but are curious about changes that could make it even better. 

Upscale
-------

![upscalers-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450188798221)

[Upscaling](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
 takes your image to the next level by enlarging its dimensions. Creative Upscale not only boosts the size but also adds subtle improvements, perfect for when your image needs that extra polish. To enlarge your image without altering it, use Subtle Upscale.

Remix
-----

![remix-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450214624525)

Remix is a powerful feature that lets you make iterations on your image by changing the prompt text. With Remix, you have the freedom to change both the prompt and the parameters you've set, allowing you to creatively steer how your images develop. Remix works a bit different on our website than on Discord, so be sure to check out our [Remix](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
 article.

The Editor
----------

Midjourney's [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
 includes Pan, Zoom Out, and Vary Region (the erase tool) all in one interface, if you'd like to make several changes at once. You can also use the individual tools on their own.

#### Pan

![pan-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450214628877)

With [Pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
, you can expand the canvas of your image in a specific direction to add more content and change its [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
.

#### Zoom Out

![zoom-out-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450214632717)

[Zoom Out](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
 gives you the ability to add more context and elements around all four sides of your original image, effectively expanding it beyond its current borders.

#### Inpainting

![vary-region-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33450214634125)

[Vary Region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
/[Erase](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32696720371341)
 is perfect for editing specific parts of your image, allowing for precise alterations without changing the rest of the image.

Use in a New Prompt
-------------------

Under Creation Actions on our website you also have the "Use" buttons which allow you to quickly and easily use your generated image as an [image prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
, [style reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
, or add the prompt text to your Imagine bar to make changes and run the prompt again.

Animate
-------

![video-header-new.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37466576182285)

The animate tools give you the ability to turn your image into a captivating 5 second video. Use the Auto buttons to jump right in, or the Manual buttons to adjust your prompt text for the video. Learn more on our [Video](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589)
 article.

Need Help Getting Started?  
  
[Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)

---

# Legacy Features – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329788681101-Legacy-Features#page-container)

Learn about legacy tools and features that shaped Midjourney's evolution.

### Discover legacy tools and features that shaped Midjourney's evolution.

If you’re curious about the older versions of Midjourney and the features they offer, you’ve come to the right place. As we keep moving forward with the latest updates, we also want to acknowledge and explore the tools and options from previous models that helped shape Midjourney to what it is today.

Legacy Versions
---------------

#### Version 5.2

Version 5.2 was released in June 2023. It was the default model from June 22, 2023 to February 14, 2024. Version 5.2 produces more detailed, sharper results with better colors, contrast, and compositions. It also has a slightly better understanding of prompts than earlier models and is more responsive to the full range of the `--stylize` parameter.

#### Version 5.1

Version 5.1 was released on May 4th, 2023. It was the default model from May 3, 2023 to June 22, 2023. Version 5.1 has a stronger default aesthetic than earlier versions, making it easier to use with simple text prompts. It also has high coherency, excels at accurately interpreting natural language prompts, produces fewer unwanted artifacts and borders, has increased image sharpness, and supports advanced features like repeating patterns with `--tile`.

#### Version 5

Version 5 was released in March 2023. It was the default model from March 30, 2023 to May 3, 2023. Version 5 produces more photographic generations than the V5.1 model, and produces images that closely match the prompt but may require longer prompts to achieve your desired aesthetic.

#### Niji 5

The Niji 5 model was released in April 2023. It can be fine-tuned with specific `--style` parameters including:  
• `--style cute` creates charming and adorable characters, props, and settings.  
• `--style expressive` has a more sophisticated illustrated feeling.  
• `--style original` uses the original Niji Model version 5, which was the default before May 26th, 2023.  
• `--style scenic` makes beautiful backgrounds and cinematic character moments in the context of their fantastical surroundings.

**Default Parameter Values**

|     | Aspect Ratio | Chaos | Quality | Seed | Stop | Stylize |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Default Value | 1:1 | 0   | 1   | random | 100 | 100 |
| Range | any | 0-100 | 0.25, 0.5, 1 | 0-4294967295 | 10-100 | 0-1000 |

  
**Upscalers:** Version 5 features the Upscale (2x) and Upscale (4x) tools, which are not compatible with [Pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
 or [Tile](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32197978340109)
. 

*   #### Version 4
    
    Version 4 was released in November 2022. It was the default model from December 20, 2022 to March 30, 2023. Version 4 is an entirely new codebase and brand-new AI architecture (compared to previous versions) designed by Midjourney and trained on the new Midjourney AI supercluster. Version 4 has more knowledge of creatures, places, objects, and more than previous versions. It's much better at getting small details right and can handle complex prompts with multiple characters or objects. Version 4 supports advanced functionality like image prompting and multi-prompts, and has very high coherency and excels with Image Prompts.  
      
    Version 4 has three slightly different "flavors" with slight tweaks to the stylistic tuning of the model. Experiment with these versions by adding `--style 4a`, `--style 4b`, or `--style 4c` to the end of a V4 prompt. 4c is the default and support aspect ratios up to 1:2 or 2:1. 4a and 4b only support 1:1, 2:3, and 3:2 aspect ratios.
    
    #### Niji 4
    
    Midjourney's first Niji model, Niji 4, was released on December 20, 2022.   
      
    **Default Parameter Values**  
    
    |     | Aspect Ratio | Chaos | Quality | Seed | Stop | Style | Stylize |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Default Value | 1:1 | 0   | 1   | random | 100 | 4c  | 100 |
    | Range | 1:2–2:1 | 0-100 | 0.25, 0.5, 1 | 0-4294967295 | 10-100 | 4a, 4b, 4c | 0-1000 |
    
      
    **Upscalers:** Earlier Midjourney model versions start by generating a grid of low-resolution image options for each Job. You can use a Midjourney upscaler on any of these images to increase the size and add additional details. The table below shows image sizes for 1:1 ratio images. For more information view our [Upscalers](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
     article.  
      
    
    | Model Version | Starting Grid | Default Upscale | Detail Upscale | Light Upscale | Beta Upscale |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Version 4 | 512 x 512px | 1024 x 1024px | 1536 x 1536px | 1536 x 1536px | 2048 x 2048px |
    | Niji 4 | 512 x 512px | 1024 x 1024px | 1024 x 1024px | 1024 x 1024px | 2048 x 2048px |
    

*   The `--test` and `--testp` models were introduced in August 2022 as part of Midjourney's effort to gather community feedback and improve upon new features. These test models allow users to explore upcoming capabilities, and they can be used alongside the `--creative` parameter for more varied compositions. When using these models, keep in mind that they support `--stylize` values ranging from 1250 to 5000, offering strong artistic influence.
    
    There are some limitations with the test models. They do not support multi-prompts or image-prompts and have a maximum aspect ratio of 3:2 or 2:3. When the aspect ratio is 1:1, they generate two initial grid images, but with other aspect ratios, they produce only one initial grid image. Additionally, in crafting prompts, note that words at the beginning of your prompt may hold more weight than those at the end. These unique characteristics make the test models an exciting option for experimental image creation.
    
    **Upscalers:** Initial grid images are 512 x 512px and the only option to upscale is Beta Upscale, which creates a 2048 x 2048px image when using 1:1 aspect ratio. For more information view our [Upscalers](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
     article.
    

*   #### Version 1
    
    Version 1 was the default model from February 2022 to April 2022. Version 1 is very abstract and painterly with low coherency.
    
    #### Version 2
    
    Version 2 was the default model from April 2022 to July 2022. Version 2 is creative, colorful, and painterly with low coherency.
    
    #### Version 3
    
    Version 3 was the default model from July 2022 to November 2022. Version 3 generates highly creative compositions with moderate coherency.  
      
    V3 Legacy Parameter: `--sameseed` Seed values create a single large random noise field applied across all images in the initial grid. When `--sameseed` is specified, all images in the initial grid use the same starting noise and will produce very similar generated images.
    
    #### High Definition
    
    `--hd` is an early alternative model that generates busy, detailed, and abstract images with low coherency.  
      
    **Upscalers:** Earlier Midjourney model versions start by generating a grid of low-resolution image options for each Job. You can use a Midjourney upscaler on any of these images to increase the size and add additional details. The table below shows image sizes for 1:1 ratio images. For more information view our [Upscalers](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32804058614669)
     article.  
      
    
    | Model Version | Starting Grid | Default (Detail) Upscale | Light Upscale | Beta Upscale | Max Upscale |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Version 1-3 | 256 x 256px | 1024 x 1024px | 1024 x 1024px | 1024 x 1024px | 1664 x 1664px |
    | hd  | 512 x 512px | 1536 x 1536px | 1536 x 1536px | 2048 x 2048px | \-- |

Legacy Upscalers
----------------

In previous Midjourney model versions, images generated at smaller sizes. You can still enlarge these images using a legacy upscaler. These tools not only increase the size but also add more details. There are various legacy upscalers you can choose from for images made with earlier models. Keep in mind, using a legacy upscaler will use [GPU minutes](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
.

#### Version 5

Midjourney model versions 5.x produce 1024 x 1024 pixel images. You can then use the `Upscale (2x)` or `Upscale (4x)` tools to increase the size of your image to 2048 x 2048 pixels or 4096 x 4096 pixels respectively. V5 upscale tools are not compatible with the [pan tool](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
 or the [tile parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32197978340109)
.

#### Versions 4 & Earlier

Each of these upscalers changes your image in different ways. All sizes are in pixels and for square aspect ratios.

| Version | Initial Image | V4 Default Upscale | Light Upscale | Beta Upscale | Detail Upscale | Max Upscale\*\* |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| V4  | 512 x 512 | 1024 x 1024 | 1536 x 1536 | 2048 x 2048 | 1536 x 1536 | \-- |
| V1-V3 | 256 x 256 | \-- | 1024 x 1024 | 1024 x 1024 | 1024 x 1024\* | 1664 x 1664 |
| Niji | 512 x 512 | 1024 x 1024 | 1024 x 1024 | 2048 x 2048 | 1024 x 1024 | \-- |
| test / testp | 512 x 512 | \-- | \-- | 2048 x 2048 | \-- | \-- |
| hd  | 512 x 512 | \-- | 1536 x 1536 | 2048 x 2048 | 1536 x 1536\* | \-- |

\* = the default upscaler for each Midjourney version model.  
\*\* Max Upscale is an older resource-intensive upscaler and is only available when users are in Fast Mode.

When using legacy versions, the `--uplight` or `--upbeta` parameters in your prompt will turn the `U#` buttons in Discord into Light Upscale or Beta Upscale shortcut buttons.

Style Tuner
-----------

The Style Tuner is a Discord feature in Midjourney version 5.2, and it set the stage for [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
. With this tool, you can use the `/tune` command along with a prompt to generate a variety of sample images. Each image showcases a different visual style based on your provided prompt. Generating these sample images uses your subscription [Fast time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
, and it can't be used in Relax Mode.

Once you pick the images you like the most, the Style Tuner gives you a special `--style code`. You can use this parameter to tailor the look of your future images, giving them a distinct style. These style code parameters can be combined and shared with other Midjourney subscribers. 

Using the `/list_tuners` command will generate a list of all of the Style Tuners you have created.

Remaster
--------

Remaster is a Discord button for upscaled images generated using legacy versions of Midjourney. It automatically [remixes your prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
 into version 5.2. Remaster any previously upscaled job by clicking the `🆕 Remaster` button beneath the upscaled image.

Stop
----

Stop is a parameter compatible with versions 6 and earlier. Using `--stop` allows you to end the image creation process before it's fully completed, resulting in softer, less detailed images.

The default stop value is 100, meaning the image completes fully unless you specify otherwise. You can choose a value between 10 to 100. This value represents the percentage of the process you'd like to stop at.

---

# Vary Region – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549-Vary-Region#page-container)

Change parts of your image while leaving the rest untouched with Vary Region in Discord.

### Perfect your image with Vary Region—select and change just a part, leaving the rest untouched!

![vary-region-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32798565981197)

What is Vary Region?
--------------------

The Vary Region tool is a feature in Discord that lets you select a part of your Midjourney-generated image and make changes to it without altering the rest of the image. It's great for fixing small mistakes, adding new elements, or making tweaks while keeping the rest of your image just as it is.

Midjourney takes the content of your original image to smartly regenerate the selected area. Whether you're refining details or experimenting with new ideas, Vary Region offers a seamless way to perfect your images.

Vary Region works with images generated in Midjourney [versions](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
 5 and later. While Vary Region is specific to Discord, you can also utilize the same tool (called Erase) on our website using the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
. 

To guide Midjourney in regenerating a specific area using Vary Region, turn on [Remix Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
 in your [Midjourney Discord settings](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517)
. Once `🎛️ Remix Mode` is active, you'll be able to edit your prompt text directly in the Vary Region editor. This helps you customize how your selected area is regenerated.

Vary Region Walkthrough
-----------------------

*   #### Generate an Image
    
    Create an image using the `/imagine` command.
    
    ![imagine-prompt-vary-region.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797165112973)
    
*   #### Upscale the Image
    
    Use the `U#` buttons to upscale your selected image.
    
    ![vary-region-upscale.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797261441037)
    
*   #### Select Vary Region
    
    Click the `🖌️ Vary (Region)` button to open the editing interface.
    
    ![vary-region-button.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797299402893)
    
*   #### Select Areas to Regenerate
    
    Choose the freehand or rectangular selection tools in the lower left of the editor and select the areas of your image that you want to regenerate.
    
    ![vary-region-select.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797367866765)
    
    The size of your selection will affect your results. Larger selections give the Midjourney Bot more room to generate new creative details. Smaller selections will result in smaller, more subtle changes. Note: You cannot edit an existing selection but can undo multiple steps using the undo button in the upper right corner.
    
*   #### Modify Your Prompt (optional)
    
    With [Remix Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32799074515213)
     turned on you can describe what you want to generate in the selected areas with an updated prompt. Your revised prompt should focus on the details you want to introduce or change.
    
    ![MJ_InPaint_NewPrompt.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797454980749)
    
*   #### Submit & View the Results
    
    Click the submit `→` button to send your request to Midjourney Bot. The Vary Region editor can now be closed, and you can return to Discord while your edit is processed.
    
    ![vary-region-submit.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797497504781)
    
    The Midjourney Bot will process your edit and generate a new image grid using the information from your original image and the guidance of your new prompt.
    
    ![vary-region-result.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32797556284813)
    
*   #### Upscale and Vary Region Again (optional)
    
    You can upscale one of your new images and use the Vary Region editor again to continue refining your image.
    

Vary Region Tips
----------------

#### Selections

The size of your selection matters! Larger selections give Midjourney more context, which can help ensure the new content matches the rest of your image. However, be careful—selecting too much might lead to new elements blending or replacing parts of the original image you wanted to keep.

#### Prompts

When using Vary Region with Remix Mode, try tweaking your prompts to focus on changes you want in the selected area. Midjourney takes the existing image into account, so short and direct prompts often work best. For instance, instead of prompting "Please change the meadow trail into a beautiful stream," be straight and prompt "meadow stream."

#### Work in Small Steps

If you want to modify several parts of an image, focus on one section at a time. This allows you to create specific prompts for each area.

*   The following [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
     are compatible with Vary Region when editing your prompt: [chaos](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32099348346765)
    , [generation speeds](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
    , [image weight](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
    , [no](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32173351982093)
    , [stylize](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
    , [style](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853)
    , [version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
    , [video](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33330535666445-Discord-Overview#h_01JH6J8BD94W2XJ91RDGV3FP52)
    , and [weird](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32390120435085)
    .

---

# Organizing Your Creations – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329462451469-Organizing-Your-Creations#page-container)

Easily manage all your Midjourney creations with the tools and features on your Organize page.

### Easily manage all your Midjourney creations with the tools and features on your Organize page!

![organize-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33732460032653)

Welcome to the [Organize page](https://www.midjourney.com/archive)
 on midjourney.com, your centralized hub for managing all your creations! 

Filters
-------

On the right side of the page you'll find a toolbar with a variety of options you can use to filter your images. Selecting filters will temporarily hide all other creations that don't match your filters.

*   **Profiles:** In the Profiles tab, you'll see all your [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
     profiles listed. Check the box next to a profile to see only the images generated using that profile. 
*   **Filters:** Ticking multiple boxes within a section displays images that match _any_ of those selections. Checking options in more than one section displays images that match _all_ of those selections. 

If it seems like some of your images are missing, it might be because a filter is applied. To view all your images again, make sure to uncheck all filter boxes.

#### View Options

These let you customize the look and layout of your Organize page

#### Timeline Bar

Next to the toolbar, you'll notice a thin gray bar resembling a scroll bar. Hovering over it reveals a timeline displaying the specific days you've generated images. Click on any date to jump straight to images created on that day.

![filters.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33520618892301)

Folders
-------

Just like on your computer, Folders let you neatly organize your images. But here's the fun part: you can now create images directly inside them!

Click the Folder icon next to the search bar to view your folders, create new ones, or create Folder Groups. Give your folders unique names and drag and drop images into them. You can also drag folders into different Folder Groups.

![folders-new.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34420593465229)

When you enter a prompt in the Imagine bar with a folder open, the results will appear right inside the folder.

The image feed of your folder will appear differently depending on whether you are viewing it from the Create page or the Organize page.

For more information, check out our [Using Folders](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/34580542725645)
 article.

Searching Your Images
---------------------

*   On the Organize page, there's a search bar at the top designed just for your personal image collection.
    
    While other parts of midjourney.com allow you to search images from other users, this search feature focuses on your own creations.
    
    You can search by using words or phrases from your prompt text, and even use [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
     like `--chaos 10` to pinpoint exactly what you're looking for.
    
*   Saved Searches (previously called Smart Folders) help you organize your images in a very easy way. With these searches, you don't need to add or remove images manually—everything sorts itself automatically based on the terms you provide.
    
    When you set up a Saved Search, only prompts that include all your search terms will appear. It doesn't matter what order the terms are in. For example, if you add "cat dog" you'll get images where both words are used in the prompt.
    
    If you want results for either word, just separate them with a comma. Keep in mind that Saved Searches will also find part of a word. So if you add "cat" you'll get results including "catapult" too.
    
    ![saved-searches.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34420599470093)
    

Bulk Actions
------------

Easily select multiple images at once by clicking and dragging or using shift + click. You can also select all the images generated on a single day by clicking the plus + icon next to the date.

After selecting, a bulk actions pop-up will appear at the bottom of your screen. This pop-up shows the number of images selected and presents several action options.

You can download images directly, or click the More button for additional actions such as adding or removing from folders, [publishing or unpublishing](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
, hiding or unhiding, and liking or unliking.

![bulk-select-tools.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33520039512077)

Hiding & Deleting Images
------------------------

Currently there isn't a way to delete images from the Midjourney website, but you can hide them if you'd like to clean up your Organize page.

Hiding an image makes it invisible to you, but it remains public and other Midjourney users can still see it. To view your hidden images, use the "hidden" checkbox filter option to reveal them.

The only way to delete images is using the ❌ emoji reaction in Discord. For more information, check out our [Discord Overview](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33330535666445)
 article.

---

# Website Overview – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329460426765-Website-Overview#page-container)

Get an overview of our website and all the tools you need to turn your ideas into stunning images.

### Welcome to midjourney.com, your gateway to endless creative possibilities!

![web-overview-header2.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33548120805133)

Our website is designed to ignite your imagination and provide all the tools you need to turn your ideas into stunning images. 

For newcomers, or if you just want a refresher on getting started, check out our [Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)
.

Explore
-------

Dive into the [Explore Page](https://www.midjourney.com/explore)
, the community gallery where you can browse a stunning array of images crafted by fellow subscribers.

![explore-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33727805313805)

With a search bar and views like Random, Hot, and Top (by day, week, or month), it's easy to find popular and trending creations.

Clicking on any image reveals details about its creator, prompt, and settings. 

Hovering over an image will give you handy shortcuts to reuse the image and prompt text in your own prompts, find similar visuals, or "like" the image. Use the Likes view to see all your liked images.

Create
------

The [Create Page](https://www.midjourney.com/imagine)
 is the heart of your image-making journey. It's where you bring your ideas to life and see your images generate in real-time.

![create-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33728439480461)

Once your creations are complete, they'll be right there for you to admire and fine-tune. This page is packed with tools and features that make it simple to continue evolving your work and modifying your images. For more detailed information, see our [Creating on Web](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390732264589)
 article.

Edit
----

The [Edit Page](https://www.midjourney.com/editor)
 is where you can access Midjourney's Editor, your gateway to uploading and editing any image using Midjourney's advanced tools.

![edit-page.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34989701132045)

For more information, see our [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
 article.

Personalize
-----------

The [Personalization Page](https://www.midjourney.com/personalize)
 is your go-to place for creating custom image styles with personalized profiles and moodboards. You can manage multiple profiles, each capturing a unique style or mood to meet your creative goals.

![personalize-page.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34990105183245)

For more information, see our [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
 article.

Organize
--------

The [Organize Page](https://www.midjourney.com/archive)
 is your hub for managing everything you create with Midjourney. You can search, filter, and sort your images to easily navigate and organize your work.

![organize-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33729837087629)

Arrange your creations using folders or explore your images by date through the Timeline Bar.

Bulk Actions make it easy to manage multiple images at once, whether you're liking, hiding, or organizing them further.

This page is all about keeping your creations organized and easily accessible. For more detailed information, see our [Organizing Your Creations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329462451469)
 article.

Rooms
-----

[Rooms](https://www.midjourney.com/rooms)
 are interactive chat spaces where creativity meets community. Access Rooms by clicking Chat in the navigation menu, and you'll find various pre-set rooms for different activities.

Join Newbies, Daily Theme, Prompt Craft for sharing prompt tips, or Help for getting your questions answered.

![rooms.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33730904244109)

You can also create your own private room by clicking the Create Room button, setting a password, and sharing the URL and password with fellow subscribers.

Inside each Room, you can chat, generate images, and even use the voice feature to talk with others, making collaboration and connection even more dynamic. 

Tasks
-----

The [Tasks page](https://www.midjourney.com/tasks)
 is where you can dive into activities that help tailor your [Personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
 profiles and potentially earn some rewards. By participating in image rankings and surveys, you contribute valuable input, helping to shape community choices and future tools.

Plus, when you complete these tasks, you may earn extra benefits like additional GPU time. For more information, see our [Complete Tasks](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390759197197)
 article.

![tasks.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34988830519309)

---

# Video – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589-Video#page-container)

Turn your images into captivating 5 second videos!

### Turn your images into captivating 5 second videos using Midjourney!

![video-header.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844248077)

Welcome to the exciting world of video creation with Midjourney! You can now turn a single image into a dynamic 5-second video.

It's as simple as feeding Midjourney an image to serve as the first frame, adding a text prompt (optional), and then watch as it brings your vision to life with a moving sequence.

• Video generation is currently only available on the midjourney.com website.  
• All plan tiers can generate videos in Fast Mode, but only Pro and Mega plans can generate videos in Relax Mode.  
• Videos cost 8x more [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
 compared to regular images (8 minutes vs 1 minute).  
• Video generations are only compatible with video-specific parameters: `--motion low`, `--motion high`, and `--raw`. 

Generating Videos
-----------------

Head to [midjourney.com](https://www.midjourney.com/imagine)
 to start creating videos! If you need help accessing our website, check out our [Logging In & Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509-Logging-In-Connecting-Accounts)
 article. 

**If you use Midjourney via Discord, please make sure you log in using the "Continue with Discord" option.**

#### **Using Midjourney Images**

All images in your gallery (regardless of what [version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853-Version)
 they were made in) now have Animate Image buttons below the Creation Actions section when you open them. You'll also see a shortcut button when you hover your mouse over them from the Create page.

![web-animate-video.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844249485)

The **Auto** buttons will automatically start generating a video using your image.

The **Manual** buttons will give you an opportunity to adjust the text prompt in the Imagine bar before generating the video.

For information on "Low Motion" and "High Motion" check out the [Video Motion](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589-Video#h_01JXZPK87W40NJP60VAR453XBZ)
 section below.

Note: Any image [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709-Parameter-List)
 used to generate your original image will be automatically removed when generating videos.

#### **Using Your Own Images**

To select an image to animate, start by clicking on the image icon ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460874798093) in the Imagine bar. This opens the images panel, allowing you to upload new images or pick from those you've already uploaded.

![video-prompt-ui.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844250637)

Click your image in the uploads library to automatically add it as a Starting Frame, or drag and drop it into the Starting Frame section. To remove your image from the Imagine bar, hover your mouse over it and click the X icon.

If you want to use your images with multiple prompts, click the lock icon ![lock-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460874802317) to keep your images pinned to the Imagine bar.

**Other Image Reference Types (not compatible with video generations):**  
![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460874803469) [Image Prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381-Image-Prompts)
  
![style-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460874804493) [Style Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
  
![character-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844253325) [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
 (replaces [Character Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293-Character-Reference)
)

*   Midjourney provides you with powerful tools for unleashing your imagination. When using our tools to create with external images, we have additional necessary precautions you should be aware of.
    
    By using external images with Midjourney, you agree to the following rules in addition to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    
    #### External Image Guidelines
    
    *   You must meet the age requirement in our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
        .
    *   You must follow all applicable laws, our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
        , and other policies.
    *   We may remove content or restrict access at our discretion.
    
    #### Your Responsibilities
    
    *   You are responsible for all content you input, create, and share.
    *   You must have the necessary rights to use the images you upload.
    *   Do not manipulate images of public or private individuals in ways that are abusive, disrespectful, offensive, derogatory, or inflammatory—this includes sexualized deepfakes.
    *   Anyone attempting to violate our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
         will face suspension or banning without refund. Use these tools with respect and consideration for others.
    
    **If you disagree with these rules, do not use Midjourney with external images.**
    
    You will likely encounter friction with our moderation — seemingly innocent prompts may be blocked by our filters. Blocked jobs don't cost you any credits. [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
     will only be deducted when you see your results.
    
    We encourage you to use this tool and your imagination with joy, wonder, responsibility, and respect.
    
    For additional information on policies, including privacy, payments, and disputes, refer to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    

Video Output
------------

Midjourney videos are generated in 480p quality, also called Standard Definition. The exact shape and size of your video is based on the aspect ratio of your starting image. If you upload your generated video to another video-sharing platform, the quality will be classified as 480p.

The table below shows how different starting image aspect ratios will affect your video's pixel dimensions:

| Starting Image Aspect Ratio | Video Aspect Ratio\* | Video Dimensions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1:1 | 1:1 | 624 x 624 pixels |
| 4:3 | 77:58 | 720 x 544 pixels |
| 2:3 | 2:3 | 512 x 768 pixels |
| 16:9 | 91:51 | 832 x 464 pixels |
| 1:2 | 1:2 | 448 x 880 pixels |

\*Midjourney may need to adjust the aspect ratio slightly in some cases. This means that your video's aspect ratio may be a little different than your starting image.

Video Settings
--------------

With an image selected as your starting frame, click the settings icon ![settings-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844254093) in the Imagine bar to access your video settings. Here you can control your default [motion setting](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589-Video#h_01JXZPK87W40NJP60VAR453XBZ)
, [GPU speed](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
, and [Stealth Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669-Stealth-Mode)
. These settings are synced with your image generation settings.

Note: Generating videos in Relax Mode is currently only available with Pro and Mega plans.

![video-settings-panel.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460844254989)

Video Playback
--------------

Once your videos have finished generating on the Create page, hover your mouse over them to play them.

You can also manually scrub (play the videos at your own speed) by holding the Control or Command key on your keyboard and moving your mouse back and forth over them. 

![scrub.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37460874809997)

Video Motion
------------

When generating videos, you have two motion settings options to choose from, "Low Motion" and "High Motion." Use the correspond buttons on the website, or add the `--motion low` or `--motion high` parameters to the end of your video prompt.

*   **Low Motion (default):** is more likely to result in still scenes, low camera motion, slow motion, or subtle character movements.
*   **High Motion:** is more likely to result in big camera motions and larger character movements, however it may also create unrealistic or glitchy movements.

Video Raw
---------

For more precise motion control of your video creations, using the `--raw` parameter in your video prompts can be helpful. This feature works similarly to [Raw Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853-Raw-Mode)
 for images.

When you add `--raw`, it reduces the extra creative flair that Midjourney usually adds, allowing your prompt text to have more influence on the outcome. 

Extend Video
------------

Video generations start at 5 seconds, but it doesn't have to stop there. After your video is created, you’ll see options to extend it further. This will add another 4 seconds to your video.

Look for the "Extend Auto" and "Extend Manual" buttons when you hover over your video on the Create page, and below the Creation Actions section when you open your video.

1.  **Extend Auto:** This button extends your video automatically, using the original prompt.
2.  **Extend Manual:** Use the manual option if you’d like to change your prompt text before extending the video. This way, you can tweak or add new elements before submitting for the longer video.

Feel free to extend your video up to 4 times, until it reaches 21 seconds, which is the maximum length available.

Download Video
--------------

When you right-click on a video from your Create or Organize page, you'll see three download options:

*   **Download for Social:** Use this option if you plan to share your videos on social media. This method uses a new optimized encoder that reduces the compression when shared on social websites, so your videos will look crisp and clear (file format is .mp4).
*   **Download Raw Video:** Use this option to download the original video file generated by Midjourney (file format is .mp4).
*   **Download Gif:** Download your video as an animated Gif (file format is .gif).

---

# Omni Reference – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997-Omni-Reference#page-container)

Put a person or object into your images using an Omni Reference.

### Want to put a person or object into your images? You can provide Midjourney with an Omni Reference!

![omni-ref-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285152349837)

What is an Omni Reference?
--------------------------

Using an Omni Reference allows you to put characters, objects, vehicles, or non-human creatures from a reference image into your Midjourney creations.

You can use it in combination with [personalization and moodboards](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
, [stylize](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
, and [style references!](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)

Omni Reference is compatible with Midjourney version 7.

• Omni Reference is not compatible with features like inpainting or outpainting that still use V6.1.  
• Using Omni Reference will cost 2x more [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
 compared to regular V7 images.  
• Omni Reference image results currently are not compatible with [vary region](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32794723105549)
, [pan](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32570788043405)
, or [zoom out](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32595476770957)
. To edit these images please load them into the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
 on midjourney.com and remove the image reference and any `--oref` or `--ow` parameters.  
• Omni Reference is currently not compatible with [Fast Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
, [Draft Mode & Conversational Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957)
, or `--q 4`.

Using an Omni Reference
-----------------------

*   To add an image to your prompt, start by clicking on the image ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285130548237) icon in the Imagine bar. This opens the images panel, allowing you to upload new images or pick from those you've already uploaded.
    
    ![omni-ref-ui.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285130549389)
    
    Drag and drop your image from the uploads library into the Omni Reference section. You can only use one image with Omni Reference. To remove your image from the Imagine bar, hover your mouse over it and click the X icon.
    
    If you want to use your images with multiple prompts, click the lock icon ![lock-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285130551437) to keep your images pinned to the Imagine bar.
    
    **Image Reference Types:**  
    ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285152370317) [Image Prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
     (default)  
    ![style-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285130552973) [Style Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
      
    ![character-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285130553229) Omni Reference (replaces [Character Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32162917505293)
    )
    
*   To use an Omni Reference in Discord, start by adding the `--oref` parameter to the end of your prompt, then pasting your image URL. You can only use one image with Omni Reference.
    
    ![discord-oref.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285152373389)
    
    It's important to ensure that you have a valid image URL, meaning the image should already be online. If your image is stored on your computer or device, you can [host it on Discord](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32558957919117)
     to generate an image URL.
    

Best Practices
--------------

*   **Importance of Text Prompts:** Combine your Omni Reference with a clear text prompt. Text is just as important for conveying the full scene and additional details beyond what the reference image shows.
*   **Reinforce the Style:** If you want your image in a different style than your reference, mention your desired style at both the start and end of your prompt. For example, "**Illustration** of a young woman with short gray hair **drawn by a comic book artist**." Also consider using [style references](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
     and lowering the [Omni Reference weight](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997-Omni-Reference#h_01JD5G8C3RY38GSHNSFH6H7H31)
    . With a lower weight you will need to reinforce the physical characteristics you want to preserve using your prompt text.
*   **Multiple Characters:** While you can only use one image as an Omni Reference, you can try using an image that contains multiple characters/people and describe them in your prompt.
*   **Account for Details:** Be aware that intricate details like specific freckles or logos on clothing may not perfectly match your reference.
*   **Consider Other Parameters:** If you're using high [stylize](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
     or `--exp` values you may want to also use a higher [Omni Reference weight](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997-Omni-Reference#h_01JD5G8C3RY38GSHNSFH6H7H31)
    , as these will all compete for influence.

*   Midjourney provides you with powerful tools for unleashing your imagination. When using our tools to create with external images, we have additional necessary precautions you should be aware of.
    
    By using external images with Midjourney, you agree to the following rules in addition to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    
    #### External Image Guidelines
    
    *   You must meet the age requirement in our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
        .
    *   You must follow all applicable laws, our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
        , and other policies.
    *   We may remove content or restrict access at our discretion.
    
    #### Your Responsibilities
    
    *   You are responsible for all content you input, create, and share.
    *   You must have the necessary rights to use the images you upload.
    *   Do not manipulate images of public or private individuals in ways that are abusive, disrespectful, offensive, derogatory, or inflammatory—this includes sexualized deepfakes.
    *   Anyone attempting to violate our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
         will face suspension or banning without refund. Use these tools with respect and consideration for others.
    
    **If you disagree with these rules, do not use Midjourney with external images.**
    
    You will likely encounter friction with our moderation — seemingly innocent prompts may be blocked by our filters. Blocked jobs don't cost you any credits. [GPU time](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
     will only be deducted when you see your results.
    
    We encourage you to use this tool and your imagination with joy, wonder, responsibility, and respect.
    
    For additional information on policies, including privacy, payments, and disputes, refer to our [Terms of Service](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32083055291277)
    .
    

Omni Reference Weight
---------------------

The Omni Reference weight parameter `--ow` allows you to control how much detail from your reference image appears in your new image. You can set this parameter to any value between 1 and 1,000, with the default being `--ow 100`.

Unless you are using a very high [stylize](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
 value, it's best to keep your weight below 400, otherwise your results may be unpredictable.

On midjourney.com you can use the slider in the Imagine bar to adjust the weight.

![omni-ref-weights.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/36285152374029)

*   • For your prompts to work, you need a text prompt in combination with your Omni Reference.  
    • Your image file should end in .png, .gif, .webp, .jpg, or .jpeg.  
    • Omni Reference can only be used with Midjourney version 7.  
    • Omni Reference can be combined with [Style References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
     and [Image Prompts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
    .

Need Help Getting Started?  
  
[Getting Started Guide](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941)

---

# Parameter List – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709-Parameter-List#page-container)

Learn how to use parameters to control, customize, and enhace your creations.

### Control, customize, and enhance your images with parameters!

What are Parameters?
--------------------

Parameters are like special instructions you can use to guide how your images turn out. They help you customize things, like changing the shape of an image, or using a [Personalization profile](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
. 

Using Parameters
----------------

Parameters always go at the end of your text prompt, after you've described what you want to see. Using them successfully is all about placement and formatting. 

![parameter-syntax.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32860748257677)

#### Remember these tips for success:

1.  **Place Parameters at the End:** Always put parameters after your prompt text.
2.  **Watch the Spaces:** Add a space between your prompt text and the dashes. 
3.  **No Punctuation:** Don't use commas, periods, or other punctuation marks in your parameters.

![thumb-down-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32861614068877) vibrant California poppies--ar 2:3  **(No space before the dashes)**  
![thumb-down-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32861614068877) vibrant California poppies - - ar 2:3  **(Extra space between the dashes)**  
![thumb-down-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32861614068877) vibrant California poppies --ar 2:3,  **(Using punctuation in parameters)**  
![thumb-down-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32861614068877) vibrant California --ar 2:3 poppies  **(Prompt text after parameters)**

Full Parameter List
-------------------

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |

# Version – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853-Version#page-container)

Switch between Midjourney's model versions using the version parameter: --version or --v

### Explore and switch between Midjourney's versions using the version parameter: `--version` or `--v`

![version-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32206880228621)

What are Versions?
------------------

Think of versions like software updates. When software is updated, it might have better graphics or new features. Similarly, Midjourney versions refer to the different models released over time—each with unique features.

Each version might handle prompts differently, have unique artistic styles, or offer improved image quality.

The current default Midjourney version is 7.

Setting a Version
-----------------

*   Add `--v #` to the end of your prompt in the Imagine bar.  
    ![web-imagine-prompt-version.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32206960222605)  
    You can choose a default version for all your images in the settings panel. To do this, click the settings ![settings-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32199847452173) button in the Imagine bar. Once you set it, this will apply to all your future prompts. 
*   Add `--v #` to the end of your prompt in Discord.  
      
    ![discord-imagine-prompt-version.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/32206981994509)  
      
    You can also set the default Version for all images using the [settings command](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32868982949517)
     and selecting one from the version dropdown menu.

Version 7
---------

Version 7 was released on April 3, 2025, and became the default model on June 17, 2025. 

In version 7 text and image prompts are handled with stunning precision, while image quality shines with richer textures and more coherent details—especially in bodies, hands, and objects.

V7 also introduces [Draft Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957)
 and [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
.

| [Quality Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32176522101773) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) (0.5, 1, 2) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) (1, 2, 4)\* |
| [Repeat Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32757107922061) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Permutations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32761322355597) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Seed Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32604356340877) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Stop Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32602768934925) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577055885197) |
| [Chaos Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32099348346765) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Raw Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Stylize Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Tile Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32197978340109) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Weird Parameter](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32390120435085) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [\--exp Parameter](https://www.midjourney.com/updates/v7-update-editor-and-exp) | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577055885197) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Niji Version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853-Version#01JDMR4T1CFVJHAF627ZVXR17A) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) --niji 6 | ![heroicons--no-symbol-16-solid.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577055885197) |
| [Relax Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Fast Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |
| [Turbo Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) | ![heroicons--check-16-solid (1).svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35577079214733) |

\* The quality parameter in V7 works differently. See more information on our [Quality](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32176522101773)
 article.

Version 6.1
-----------

Version 6.1 was released on July 30, 2024, and was the default model until June 16, 2025. It produces more coherent images with more precise details and textures, and generates images approximately 25% faster than version 6.

Version 6
---------

Version 6 was released on December 20, 2023, and was the default model from February 14 to July 30, 2024. Version 6 has enhanced prompt accuracy for longer inputs, improved coherence and knowledge, and advanced image prompting and remixing capabilities.

Niji 6
------

_Niji models are a special series within Midjourney, developed in collaboration with Spellbrush, to focus on Eastern and anime aesthetics and illustrative styles. Niji models have their own dedicated [website](https://nijijourney.com/home)
 and [Discord server](https://discord.com/invite/nijijourney)
, providing a tailored experience for anime enthusiasts._

The Niji 6 model, released on June 7, 2024, features improved rendering of Japanese text, handling short Japanese kana text effectively and even rendering simple Chinese characters. It offers better image detail, particularly in elements like the structure of anime eyes, and addresses certain minor image artifacts that affected a small number of previous generations.

For information about older versions, please see our [Legacy Features](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329788681101)
 article.

---
