# Creating on Web – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390732264589-Creating-on-Web#page-container)

Explore all the tools and features on your Create page and watch your images generate in real time.

### Unleash your creativity on the Create page!

![create-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35592155883661)

Welcome to the [Create page](https://www.midjourney.com/imagine)
 on midjourney.com, your hub for generating amazing images! While you can use the Imagine bar on many pages, the Create page is where you can watch your images come to life right in front of your eyes. 

Imagine Bar
-----------

The Imagine bar is where you type your prompts. Hit the send button or press enter on your keyboard, and your images will start generating.

You'll find several helpful tools in the Imagine bar—one for adding images ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540577307789), another to change your default settings ![settings-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35113668799629), and one to manage your [personalization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
 settings ![p-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35592155884429). Also in the Imagine bar is ![draft-mode-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35592155885069) Draft Mode, which allows you to prototype images at half the GPU cost. Check out our [Draft Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957)
 article for more information.

Next to the Imagine bar is a search box, where you can quickly search all the prompts in your creation history.

Hold Ctrl (or Cmd on Mac) and hit Enter. This runs your prompt and keeps the text in the Imagine bar, so you can easily use the prompt again.

#### Images Panel

Click the image ![image-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540577307789) icon, and you'll get instant access to your images panel. This is your go-to spot for uploading new images to Midjourney or picking from your uploads library to enhance your prompt.

![web-ui-image-prompt-v7.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37435702801805)

Hover over any image in your uploads library, and you'll see three shortcut buttons pop up.

*   Click the "i" ![describe-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540577313293) icon to run [Describe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32497889043981)
    , which suggest prompt text to match your image.
*   Use the pencil ![pencil-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540577321229) icon to open your image in the [Editor](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32764383466893)
    .
*   Press the trash can ![trash-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540570609421) icon to delete an image from your uploads library. You can also do this on your [Manage Uploads](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329380893325)
     page.

When you open the images panel, two extra buttons appear on the Imagine bar.

*   Use the lock ![lock-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540570621709) icon to secure your chosen images in the Imagine bar, so you can quickly use them again in another prompt.
*   Click the trash can ![trash-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33540570609421) icon to remove all images from the Imagine bar.

Drag your image into the Imagine bar and drop it into your desired section:

*   Use the image as an [Image Prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
     ![image-prompt-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33541483470605) (the default option).
*   Use your image as a [Style Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
     ![style-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33541483475085) to capture a specific look.
*   Use your image as a [Omni Reference](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997)
    ![character-reference-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33541493528589) to maintain character consistency.

#### Settings Panel

When you click the settings icon, you can adjust the default settings that will automatically apply to all your prompts.

![web-settings.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33541185010701)

*   **Image Size:** Change your default [aspect ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
     to fit your vision perfectly.
*   **Model:**
    *   Toggle [Raw Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853)
         on or off for different image effects.
    *   Choose your default [Midjourney version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
         for generating images.
    *   Turn [Draft Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957)
         on for quick prototyping.
*   **Aesthetics:**
    *   Play with [Stylization](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
         to influence how artistically your images are rendered.
    *   Adjust [Weirdness](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32390120435085)
         to add unique quirks.
    *   Control [Variety](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32099348346765)
         for more diverse outputs.
*   **More Options:**
    *   Select your default [GPU speed](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
        .
    *   Activate [Stealth Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
         if your plan allows, keeping your creations private.

Creation Feed
-------------

The central feature of the Create page is the creation feed. Here, you can watch your images generate in real-time and revisit all your finished creations.

When you hover your mouse over any image in the feed, shortcut buttons pop up that let you quickly create either [subtle or strong variations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32692978437005)
 of that image.

To the right of the images, you'll see the [prompt text](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32023408776205)
, [parameters](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32859204029709)
, and reference images that were used to generate your images. Hover over this section to access more shortcut buttons.

With these, you can ![rerun-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33542595521549) **Rerun** the same prompt immediately, ![use-text-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33542595525645) **Use** the prompt text and images for a new creation, ![hide-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33542595528333) **Hide** images from your feed (with the option to unhide on your [Organize page](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329462451469)
), or explore ![more-options-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33542595531789) **More** options. 

![creation-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33543851978509)

Creating in Folders
-------------------

When you're on the Create page, you'll see a folder button right next to the search bar at the top. Clicking this reveals all your Folders and Folder Groups.

![folders-new.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34443635184397)

If you click a folder to open it, you'll see a dedicated creation space just for that folder, and you can generate images directly inside it! 

![create-in-folders.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34443621870349)

Ready to leave a folder? Just click the X in the folder button next to the search bar.

For more information about folders, check out our [Using Folders](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/34580542725645)
 article.

More Image Options
------------------

When you click on an image from your creation feed it will open fullscreen, giving you more options and tools.

At the top, near the prompt text, you'll find a toolbar packed with useful features.

![image-options-tools.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33545538983693)

The More Options ![options-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33544752808589) button lets you copy important details like the [Prompt](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32023408776205)
, [Job ID](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32635695384461)
, [Seed](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32604356340877)
, Image, or Image URL. You can report any image that violates our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
, choose to [Publish or Unpublish](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
, Download, Hide or Unhide it, and even open it in Discord (if it was created there).

Next to this, you'll find icons to Download the image, Search our community for similar images, and mark your favorites with a Like.

Above the Creation Actions, there's a folder ![folder-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34443635188109) icon. If your image is already in a folder, you'll see the folder name right there. If not, you can click the folder icon to quickly add the image to a folder.

In the Creation Actions section, you can further tweak your images and continue working with them. For a full breakdown of all these tools and features, check out our [Modifying Your Creations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329329805581)
 article.

---

# Getting Started Guide – Midjourney

[Skip to main content](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329261836941-Getting-Started-Guide#page-container)

Learn to subscribe, create your first image, explore features, and connect with our creative community.

### Welcome to Midjourney, your portal to transforming text into amazing images! If you're ready to unleash your creativity, this guide is your first step to crafting stunning images and exploring endless possibilities.

![getting-started-header.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/33551418522253)

Subscribing to Midjourney
-------------------------

Before you dive into creating your first masterpiece, you'll need to subscribe to one of our plans. Here's how you can get started:

*   Log In to midjourney.com: [Logging In & Connecting Accounts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390994570509)
    
*   Select a Plan: [Comparing Midjourney Plans](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/27870484040333)
    
*   Subscribe: [How to Subscribe](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31974654274573)
    

Making Your First Image
-----------------------

Check out this video for a quick introduction to using Midjourney, then follow the guide below to create your first images!

1.  **Visit Your Create Page:** Go to the [Create](https://www.midjourney.com/imagine)
     page on midjourney.com. This is where your images come to life, and you can see them appear in real-time.
2.  **Use the Imagine Bar:** At the top of the page, you'll see the Imagine bar. Here, type what you'd like to see—this is your prompt.   
    ![imagine-prompt-bar.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37435945755533)
3.  **Generate Your Image:** After pressing Enter or the send button if you're using a mobile device, Midjourney creates a set of four images. Watch as your images take form.
4.  **Congratulations!** Once it reaches 100%, you're done! You've created your first Midjourney images. 

![create-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37435945762573)

Writing and crafting prompts can be an art in and of itself. To learn more, check out our [Prompt Basics](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32023408776205)
 and [Art of Prompting](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32835253061645)
 articles.

Personalize Midjourney
----------------------

Midjourney is even better when [personalized](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32433330574221)
. Create moodboards and custom personalization profiles that will help Midjourney generate images that uniquely match your individual style!

![personalize-page.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/35592870713485)

Continue Working on Your Images
-------------------------------

The creativity doesn't stop here! Learn how to enhance and refine your creations using upscalers, variations, zoom out, pan, editor, and more in our [Modifying Your Creations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329329805581)
 article.

![modify-images.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37435945765389)

Turn Images into Videos
-----------------------

Make your images come alive by transforming them into 5 second videos! Learn how to animate both your Midjourney creations and your own images on our [Video](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/37460773864589)
 article.

![video-header-new.gif](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37465655295245)

Customizing Your Settings
-------------------------

You can change your default image generation settings at any time by clicking on the settings icon ![settings-icon.svg](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34106580885389) in the Imagine bar.

![web-settings.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34106580894477)

For more information on each setting, check out these articles: [Aspect Ratio](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/31894244298125)
 (image size), [Raw Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32634113811853)
, [Version](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32199405667853)
, [Draft Mode](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/35577175650957)
, [Stylize](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32196176868109)
, [Weird](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32390120435085)
, [Variety](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32099348346765)
, [GPU Speed](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32016412137741)
, and [Stealth](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32019750070669)
.

Using Images in Your Prompts
----------------------------

Did you know that you can also provide Midjourney with images—not just text—to guide your creations?

*   [Image Prompts](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32040250122381)
     let you influence content, composition, style, and colors.
*   [Style References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32180011136653)
     help you match the look and feel of another image.
*   [Omni References](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/36285124473997-Omni-Reference)
     help you use the same character or object in multiple images.

![omni-ref-ui.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/37435936953741)

For more information about all the tools and features available on your Create page, check out our [Creating on Web](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33390732264589)
 article.

Organizing Your Creations
-------------------------

Your Organize page offers a clear view of all your Midjourney images. Here, you can download, sort, and filter your creations. You can also organize them into folders easily. For more tips and tricks, check out our [Organizing Your Creations](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/33329462451469)
 article.

![organize-feed.png](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/article_attachments/34106580896909)

Collaborating
-------------

Nothing beats the creative energy that comes from making images with others!

On the [Chat page](https://www.midjourney.com/rooms)
, you can find (or create!) shared spaces to work together with other subscribers.

The [Explore page](https://www.midjourney.com/explore)
 is another great resource for inspiration—it's a showcase of subscriber creations!

Check out the [Daily Theme](https://www.midjourney.com/rooms/fdcd697e-d8c9-4848-9d6b-27dc8a209eea)
 room every day to see the creative ways other users are incorporating the day's theme into prompts, and create alongside them. 

Community Guidelines
--------------------

To ensure a safe and happy creative environment, stay informed about our [Community Guidelines](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32013696484109)
.

Sharing & Support
-----------------

Feel like sharing your works of art? Connect with our community and seek guidance from fellow Midjourney enthusiasts or our helpers in [our Discord server](https://discord.gg/midjourney)
.

If you need help with your account or subscription, you can browse helpful [billing articles](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/categories/16016577793421)
 or [contact our billing team](https://docs.midjourney.com/hc/en-us/articles/32638309968141)
.

---
